  - id: 17
    date: 31/10/2025
    title: "Happy Halloween!"
    content: |-
      It's the 31st, and you know what that means! Happy All Hallows' Eve everyone! A few changes occured:

      1. I merged the blogs page back into index.html, providing a smoother experience with the tab bar.
      2. Projects have been moved to the now Projects tab, and it has multiple sections, currently: Coding Projects, Books, and Minecraft.
      3. I have added back the fuctionality of using # to define where you want to be! Now you can add **#about**, **#blog**, or **#projects** at the end of the link to be on the Profile, Blog, or Projects tab respectively. Furthermore, blogs now had a numerical ID, displayed next to the date. With **#blog?id={ID}** where **{ID}** is the ID of the blog post, you can directly open to page to that post!
      4. Now practically everything are now defined using JSON, e.g. the blog posts, projects, even the books! This makes my life SO much easier making these posts and stuff, and makes my code just that tad bit cleaner and shorter! Hopefully because of this, I'll be making more blog posts now!
      5. As a Halloween special, I'm making a 3 chapter short psychological horror story that may release in a few weeks.
      6. Also, I've added back the [RSS feed](~/&id=8) feature!

      Anyways, that's all for now, have a very happy Halloween guys!

  - id: 9
    date: 12/03/2025
    title: "UI & Features Revamp"
    content: |-
      The entire website has now just been revamped! As you can see, everything looks more fresh and heck, more modern! I'll let you explore that on your own.

      Now onto the features!

      First of all, I added a contact me form on the main page, so you guys can send me emails from this very website! I also added a newsletter feed under it, you just plop your email there and BOOM!, you're subscribed!

      Secondly, the blog post "jump to tags" function has also been changed. As you can see above the big blog titles, there's a small line of text that contains the blog number and the blog date. The jump to tags now function using the blog number. The format is **#blog<#|-** with **<#|-** being the blog number. For example, to automatically jump to this blog post, you would go to **https://devicals.github.io/blogs#9**, note the main part: **#blog9**. Also, to view the latest blog post, you can now go to the tag **#blog0**!

      Alright, that's it for now, see y'all! (It has since been revamped again, twice!)

<!DOCTYPE html>

    <meta charset="UTF-8">

    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Fira+Code:wght@300;400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="extra/style.css">
    <style>
        :root {
            --background: 246 13% 30%;
            --foreground: 0 0% 98%;
            --card: 246 13% 25%;
            --card-foreground: 0 0% 98%;
            --primary: 0 0% 98%;
            --primary-foreground: 246 13% 30%;
            --secondary: 246 13% 20%;
            --secondary-foreground: 0 0% 98%;
            --muted: 246 13% 20%;
            --muted-foreground: 240 5% 64.9%;
            --accent: 342 82% 73%;
            --accent-foreground: 0 0% 98%;
            --border: 246 13% 40%;
            --input: 246 13% 20%;
            --ring: 342 82% 73%;
            --radius: 0rem;
        }

        * {
            margin: 0;
            padding: 0;
            box-sizing: border-box;
        }

        body {
            font-family: 'Fira Code', monospace;
            background-color: hsl(var(--background));
            color: hsl(var(--foreground));
            min-height: 100vh;
            padding: 20px;
        }

        .container {
            max-width: 900px;
            margin: 0 auto;
        }

        header {
            text-align: center;
            margin-bottom: 40px;
        }

        h1 {
            font-size: 2.5rem;
            font-weight: 700;
            margin-bottom: 10px;
        }

        .text-accent {
            color: hsl(var(--accent));
        }

        .subtitle {
            color: hsl(var(--muted-foreground));
            font-size: 0.875rem;
        }

        .card {
            background-color: hsl(var(--card) / 0.5);
            backdrop-filter: blur(12px);
            border: 1px solid hsl(var(--border) / 0.5);
            border-radius: calc(var(--radius));
            padding: 24px;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
            box-shadow: 0 4px 6px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
        }

        h2 {
            font-size: 1.5rem;
            font-weight: 700;
            margin-bottom: 20px;
            color: hsl(var(--foreground));

            <script>
                async function fetchGitHubLanguageStats() {
                try {
                    const response = await fetch('https://api.github.com/repos/devicals/devicals.github.io/languages');

                    if (!response.ok) {
                    throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
                    }

                    const languages = await response.json();
                    const totalBytes = Object.values(languages).reduce((sum, bytes) => sum + bytes, 0);

                    const languageStats = Object.entries(languages)
                    .map(([language, bytes]) => ({
                        language,
                        percentage: ((bytes / totalBytes) * 100).toFixed(1)
                    }))
                    .sort((a, b) => parseFloat(b.percentage) - parseFloat(a.percentage));

                    const statsString = languageStats
                    .map(({ language, percentage }) => `${language}: ${percentage}%`)
                    .join(', ');

                    return statsString;

                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('Error fetching GitHub language stats:', error);
                    return 'HTML: 95.1%, JS: 0.2%, CSS: 4.7%';
                }
                }

                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', updateLanguageStats);
            </script>
        </div>

        <footer>

        </footer>

    <script>
        const container = document.getElementById('items-container');
        for (let i = 1; i <= 9; i++) {
            const group = document.createElement('div');
            group.className = 'input-group';
            group.innerHTML = `
                <div class="input-row">
                    <div>
                        <label for="i${i}">Item ${i}:</label>
                        <input type="text" id="i${i}" placeholder="e.g., minecraft:stick" oninput="validateInput(this); updateDataState(${i})">
                    </div>
                    <div>
                        <label for="d${i}">Item ${i} Custom Data:</label>
                        <input type="text" id="d${i}" placeholder="e.g., custom:data" disabled oninput="validateInput(this)">
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            container.appendChild(group);
        }

        function validateInput(input) {
            const regex = /^[a-z_:\/]*$/;
            if (!regex.test(input.value)) {
                input.value = input.value.replace(/[^a-z_:\/]/g, '');
            }
        }

        function updateDataState(itemNum) {
            const itemInput = document.getElementById(`i${itemNum}`);
            const dataInput = document.getElementById(`d${itemNum}`);

            if (itemInput.value.trim() === '') {
                dataInput.disabled = true;
                dataInput.value = '';
            } else {
                dataInput.disabled = false;
            }
        }

        function generate() {
            const items = [];
            const data = [];
            const dataBools = [];
            const isAir = [];

            for (let i = 1; i <= 9; i++) {
                const itemVal = document.getElementById(`i${i}`).value.trim();
                const dataVal = document.getElementById(`d${i}`).value.trim();

                items.push(itemVal);
                data.push(dataVal);
                dataBools.push(dataVal !== '' ? '1' : '0');
                isAir.push(itemVal === '' ? '1' : '0');
            }

            const result = document.getElementById('res').value.trim();

            const output = `function cc:mystic_table/recipe/base_recipe {item_0:${items[0]},item_1:${items[1]},item_2:${items[2]},item_3:${items[3]},item_4:${items[4]},item_5:${items[5]},item_6:${items[6]},item_7:${items[7]},item_8:${items[8]},data_0:"${data[0]}",data_1:"${data[1]}",data_2:"${data[2]}",data_3:"${data[3]}",data_4:"${data[4]}",data_5:"${data[5]}",data_6:"${data[6]}",data_7:"${data[7]}",data_8:"${data[8]}",0:${dataBools[0]},1:${dataBools[1]},2:${dataBools[2]},3:${dataBools[3]},4:${dataBools[4]},5:${dataBools[5]},6:${dataBools[6]},7:${dataBools[7]},8:${dataBools[8]},result:"${result}",is_air_0:${isAir[0]},is_air_1:${isAir[1]},is_air_2:${isAir[2]},is_air_3:${isAir[3]},is_air_4:${isAir[4]},is_air_5:${isAir[5]},is_air_6:${isAir[6]},is_air_7:${isAir[7]},is_air_8:${isAir[8]}}`;

            document.getElementById('output-text').textContent = output;
            document.getElementById('output-card').classList.add('show');
            document.getElementById('output-card').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
        }

        function copyToClipboard() {
            const text = document.getElementById('output-text').textContent;
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(() => {
                const btn = event.target;
                const originalText = btn.textContent;
                btn.textContent = '✓ Copied!';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    btn.textContent = originalText;
                }, 2000);
            });
        }
    </script>

            wrapper.querySelectorAll('.tag-box').forEach(tag => {
                tag.style.setProperty('--rand-z', `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 50) + 30}px`);
                tag.style.setProperty('--rand-y', `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 12) * -1}px`);
                tag.style.setProperty('--rand-r', `${Math.floor(Math.random() * 24) - 12}deg`);
            });
        }

        function handleTilt(e) {
            const wrapper = e.currentTarget;
            const card = wrapper.querySelector('.fav-card, .interest-grid-card');
            const rect = wrapper.getBoundingClientRect();
            const clientX = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
            const clientY = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;
            const x = clientX - rect.left, y = clientY - rect.top;
            const centerX = rect.width / 2, centerY = rect.height / 2;
            let rotX, rotY, scale;
            if (card.classList.contains('fav-card')) {
                rotX = Math.max(Math.min((centerY - y) / 15, 7), -7);
                rotY = Math.max(Math.min((x - centerX) / 80, 7), -7);
                scale = 1.03;
            } else {
                rotX = (centerY - y) / 6; rotY = (x - centerX) / 10; scale = 1.1;
            }
            card.style.transform = `rotateX(${rotX}deg) rotateY(${rotY}deg) scale3d(${scale}, ${scale}, ${scale})`;
        }

        function createTiltWrapper(contentClass, innerHTML) {
            const wrap = document.createElement('div');
            wrap.className = 'tilt-wrapper';
            wrap.innerHTML = `<div class="${contentClass}">${innerHTML}</div>`;
            const start = () => { if (contentClass === 'fav-card') randomizeTags(wrap); wrap.classList.add('is-tapped'); };
            wrap.addEventListener('mouseenter', start);
            wrap.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => { document.querySelectorAll('.is-tapped').forEach(w => w.classList.remove('is-tapped')); start(); handleTilt(e); }, {passive: true});
            wrap.addEventListener('mousemove', handleTilt);
            wrap.addEventListener('touchmove', handleTilt, {passive: true});
            wrap.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => { wrap.querySelector('div').style.transform = `rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) scale3d(1,1,1)`; wrap.classList.remove('is-tapped'); });
            return wrap;
        }

        function fitText(el) {
            let fs = 0.85; el.style.fontSize = fs + 'rem';
            while (el.scrollHeight > el.offsetHeight && fs > 0.5) { fs -= 0.02; el.style.fontSize = fs + 'rem'; }
        }

        async function initAuth() {
            const { data: { session } } = await supabaseClient.auth.getSession();
            handleUserSession(session);
            supabaseClient.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
                handleUserSession(session);
            });
        }

        function handleUserSession(session) {
            if (session && session.user && session.user.email.toLowerCase() === '3rr0r.d3v@gmail.com') {
                isAdmin = true;
                document.body.classList.add('is-admin');
            } else {
                isAdmin = false;
                document.body.classList.remove('is-admin');
            }
            if (interestsData) renderPage();
        }

        async function syncToSupabase() {
            if (!isAdmin) return;
            const { error } = await supabaseClient
                .from('site_content')
                .update({ data: { favorites: interestsData.favorites, sections: [] } })
                .eq('key', contentKey);
            if (error) {
                alert("Error saving: " + error.message);
            }
        }

        async function loadSpotifySongs() {
            try {
                const resp = await fetch('/music.json');
                const json = await resp.json();
                if (json && json[0] && json[0].tracks) {
                    const rawTracks = json[0].tracks;
                    const seenIds = new Set();
                    spotifyTracks = rawTracks.filter(t => {
                        if (seenIds.has(t.id)) return false;
                        seenIds.add(t.id);
                        return true;
                    });
                }
            } catch(e) {
                console.error(e);
            }
        }

        async function init() {
            await loadSpotifySongs();

            const { data, error } = await supabaseClient
                .from('site_content')
                .select('data')
                .eq('key', contentKey)
                .single();

            if (data && data.data) {
                interestsData = data.data;
                renderPage();
            } else if (error && error.code === 'PGRST116') {
                if (isAdmin) {
                    interestsData = { 
                        favorites: [], 
                        sections: [] 
                    };
                    await supabaseClient
                        .from('site_content')
                        .insert({ key: contentKey, data: interestsData });
                    renderPage();
                } else {
                    document.getElementById('interests-content').innerHTML = `
                        <p style="color: hsl(var(--muted-foreground)); font-style: italic; text-align: center; margin-top: 50px;">This interest page is currently empty.</p>
                    `;
                }
            }

            supabaseClient
                .channel('interests-realtime')
                .on(
                    'postgres_changes',
                    { event: 'UPDATE', schema: 'public', table: 'site_content', filter: `key=eq.${contentKey}` },
                    (payload) => {
                        if (payload.new && payload.new.data) {
                            interestsData = payload.new.data;
                            renderPage();
                        }
                    }
                )
                .subscribe();

            await initAuth();
        }

        function renderPage() {
            const container = document.getElementById('interests-content');
            container.innerHTML = '';

            if (interestsData.favorites) {
                const sec = document.createElement('div');
                sec.className = 'interest-outer';
                sec.innerHTML = `
                    <h2 class="interest-title">Favorites</h2>
                    <button class="admin-section-btn" onclick="openAddFavModal()">+ Add Favorite</button>
                    <div class="interest-fav-list" id="fav-list-container"></div>
                `;
                const list = sec.querySelector('.interest-fav-list');
                
                interestsData.favorites.forEach((fav, idx) => {
                    let tagsHTML = '';
                    const tagList = fav.tags || [];
                    tagList.forEach(t => { tagsHTML += `<span class="tag-box tag-${t.style || 'accent'}">${t.tag}</span>`; });
                    
                    const inner = `
                        <button class="admin-action-btn" id="edit-fav-btn-${idx}" style="top:4px; left:4px;">✎</button>
                        <button class="admin-action-btn del-btn" id="del-fav-btn-${idx}" style="top:4px; right:4px;">✕</button>
                        <div class="fav-info-group">
                            <div class="fav-title">${fav.title}</div>
                            <span class="fav-comment">${fav.comment || ''}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="fav-tags">${tagsHTML}</div>
                    `;
                    
                    const wrap = createTiltWrapper('fav-card', inner);
                    wrap.dataset.index = idx;

                    if (isAdmin) {
                        wrap.draggable = true;
                        wrap.addEventListener('dragstart', (e) => {
                            dragItemIdx = idx;
                            dragCategory = 'favorites';
                            e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
                        });
                        wrap.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
                            if (dragCategory !== 'favorites') return;
                            e.preventDefault();
                        });
                        wrap.addEventListener('drop', async (e) => {
                            if (dragCategory !== 'favorites') return;
                            e.preventDefault();
                            const targetIdx = idx;
                            if (dragItemIdx === targetIdx) return;
                            const [reorderedItem] = interestsData.favorites.splice(dragItemIdx, 1);
                            interestsData.favorites.splice(targetIdx, 0, reorderedItem);
                            await syncToSupabase();
                        });
                    }

                    list.appendChild(wrap);

                    const delBtn = document.getElementById(`del-fav-btn-${idx}`);
                    if (delBtn) {
                        delBtn.onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); deleteFavorite(idx); };
                    }

                    const editBtn = document.getElementById(`edit-fav-btn-${idx}`);
                    if (editBtn) {
                        editBtn.onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); openEditFavModal(fav, idx); };
                    }
                });
                container.appendChild(sec);
            }

            const sec = document.createElement('div');
            sec.className = 'interest-outer';
            sec.innerHTML = `
                <h2 class="interest-title">Music I Drank</h2>
                <div class="interest-grid" id="grid-container-spotify"></div>
            `;
            const grid = sec.querySelector('.interest-grid');
            
            spotifyTracks.forEach((track) => {
                const inner = `
                    ${track.title}
                    <span class="tooltip-text">${track.artists.join(', ')}</span>
                `;
                const wrap = createTiltWrapper('interest-grid-card tooltip-container', inner);
                const card = wrap.querySelector('.interest-grid-card');
                if (card) {
                    card.onclick = () => window.open(`https://open.spotify.com/track/${track.id}`, '_blank');
                }
                grid.appendChild(wrap);
            });
            container.appendChild(sec);

            document.querySelectorAll('.interest-grid-card').forEach(fitText);
        }

        window.openAddFavModal = () => {
            activeEditIdx = null;
            document.getElementById('fav-title-input').value = '';
            document.getElementById('fav-comment-input').value = '';
            document.getElementById('tag-0-text').value = '';
            document.getElementById('tag-0-style').value = 'accent';
            document.getElementById('tag-1-text').value = '';
            document.getElementById('tag-1-style').value = 'accent';
            document.getElementById('fav-modal').classList.add('active');
        };

        function openEditFavModal(fav, idx) {
            activeEditIdx = idx;
            document.getElementById('fav-title-input').value = fav.title;
            document.getElementById('fav-comment-input').value = fav.comment || '';
            const tag0 = fav.tags?.[0] || { tag: '', style: 'accent' };
            const tag1 = fav.tags?.[1] || { tag: '', style: 'accent' };
            document.getElementById('tag-0-text').value = tag0.tag;
            document.getElementById('tag-0-style').value = tag0.style;
            document.getElementById('tag-1-text').value = tag1.tag;
            document.getElementById('tag-1-style').value = tag1.style;
            document.getElementById('fav-modal').classList.add('active');
        }

        window.closeFavModal = () => {
            document.getElementById('fav-modal').classList.remove('active');
        };

        window.saveFavorite = async () => {
            const title = document.getElementById('fav-title-input').value.trim();
            const comment = document.getElementById('fav-comment-input').value.trim();
            if (!title) return;

            const tags = [];
            const tag0Text = document.getElementById('tag-0-text').value.trim();
            const tag1Text = document.getElementById('tag-1-text').value.trim();
            if (tag0Text) tags.push({ tag: tag0Text, style: document.getElementById('tag-0-style').value });
            if (tag1Text) tags.push({ tag: tag1Text, style: document.getElementById('tag-1-style').value });

            const favObj = { title, comment, tags };
            if (activeEditIdx !== null) {
                musicData.favorites[activeEditIdx] = favObj;
            } else {
                if (!musicData.favorites) musicData.favorites = [];
                musicData.favorites.push(favObj);
            }
            closeFavModal();
            await syncToSupabase();
        };

        async function deleteFavorite(idx) {
            if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to delete this favorite?`)) return;
            interestsData.favorites = interestsData.favorites.filter((_, i) => i !== idx);
            await syncToSupabase();
        }

        document.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
            if (!e.target.closest('.tilt-wrapper')) document.querySelectorAll('.is-tapped').forEach(w => w.classList.remove('is-tapped'));
        }, {passive: true});

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

(CONTENT END)

      .tl-item.revived { background: rgba(255,230,80,0.10); border-color: rgba(255,220,50,0.3); }

  <script>
    const PRESET_COLORS = ['#FF3B3B','#FF6B3B','#FF9A3B','#FFD93B','#A8D63F','#3FD67A','#3FBDD6','#3F7ED6','#7B5EA7','#5A4080','#3D2B60','#4A4A4A','#2E2E2E','#1A1A1A','#8B0000','#C0392B','#E67E22','#27AE60','#2980B9','#8E44AD','#2C3E50','#ECF0F1'];

    const TIERS_BASE = [
      { id:'SSS',  label:'SSS',       color:'#FF3B3B', text:'#fff',    isExec:false },
      { id:'SS',   label:'SS',        color:'#FF6B3B', text:'#fff',    isExec:false },
      { id:'S',    label:'S',         color:'#FF9A3B', text:'#fff',    isExec:false },
      { id:'A',    label:'A',         color:'#FFD93B', text:'#2a1a00', isExec:false },
      { id:'B',    label:'B',         color:'#A8D63F', text:'#1a2a00', isExec:false },
      { id:'C',    label:'C',         color:'#3FD67A', text:'#003020', isExec:false },
      { id:'D',    label:'D',         color:'#3FBDD6', text:'#002030', isExec:false },
      { id:'E',    label:'E',         color:'#3F7ED6', text:'#fff',    isExec:false },
      { id:'F',    label:'F',         color:'#7B5EA7', text:'#fff',    isExec:false },
      { id:'FF',   label:'FF',        color:'#5A4080', text:'#fff',    isExec:false },
      { id:'FFF',  label:'FFF',       color:'#3D2B60', text:'#ccc',    isExec:false },
      { id:'Z',    label:'Z',         color:'#4A4A4A', text:'#fff',    isExec:false },
      { id:'ZZ',   label:'ZZ',        color:'#2E2E2E', text:'#aaa',    isExec:false },
      { id:'ZZZ',  label:'ZZZ',       color:'#1A1A1A', text:'#777',    isExec:false },
      { id:'Q',    label:'Q',         color:'#b53333', text:'#ffcccc', isExec:true  },
      { id:'EXEC', label:'EXECUTION', color:'#8B0000', text:'#ff6b6b', isExec:true  },
    ];

    let PRESETS = {};
    let PRESET_LIST = [];

    const AUTOSAVE_KEY = 'tierlist_autosave';
    const SAVES_KEY    = 'tierlist_saves';

    let allTiers      = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(TIERS_BASE));
    let activeTierIds = TIERS_BASE.map(t => t.id);
    let columns       = 1;
    let tierItems     = {};
    let poolItems     = [];
    let idCounter     = 0;
    let revivalTint   = false;
    let revivedSet    = new Set();

    function getTier(id)      { return allTiers.find(t => t.id === id); }
    function getActiveTiers() { return activeTierIds.map(id => getTier(id)).filter(Boolean); }
    function isExecTier(id)   { const t = getTier(id); return t && t.isExec; }

    function parseRankingDat(yaml) {
      const lines = yaml.split(/\r?\n/);
      const presets = [];
      let current = null, inTiers = false;
      for (const raw of lines) {
        const line = raw.trimEnd(), trimmed = line.trim();
        if (!trimmed || trimmed.startsWith('#')) continue;
        if (trimmed === 'presets:') continue;
        if (/^  - id:/.test(line)) {
          if (current) presets.push(current);
          current = { id: trimmed.replace('- id:', '').trim(), label: '', tiers: [] };
          inTiers = false;
        } else if (current && /^    label:/.test(line)) {
          current.label = trimmed.replace('label:', '').trim();
          inTiers = false;
        } else if (current && /^    tiers:/.test(line)) {
          inTiers = true;
        } else if (current && inTiers && /^      - /.test(line)) {
          current.tiers.push(trimmed.replace('- ', '').trim());
        }
      }
      if (current) presets.push(current);
      return presets;
    }

    async function loadRankingDat() {
      try {
        const resp = await fetch('ranking.dat');
        if (!resp.ok) throw new Error('not found');
        const yaml = await resp.text();
        const parsed = parseRankingDat(yaml);
        PRESET_LIST = parsed.map(p => ({
          id: p.id,
          label: p.label,
          tierIds: p.tiers.map(lbl => TIERS_BASE.find(t => t.label === lbl)?.id).filter(Boolean),
        }));
        PRESETS = {};
        for (const p of PRESET_LIST) PRESETS[p.id] = p.tierIds;
      } catch(e) {
        PRESET_LIST = [
          { id:'standard', label:'Standard', tierIds: ['S','A','B','C','D','F'].map(lbl => TIERS_BASE.find(t => t.label === lbl)?.id).filter(Boolean) },
          { id:'full',     label:'Full',     tierIds: TIERS_BASE.map(t => t.id) },
        ];
        PRESETS = {};
        for (const p of PRESET_LIST) PRESETS[p.id] = p.tierIds;
      }
      buildPresetSelector();
    }

    function buildPresetSelector() {
      const sel = document.getElementById('presetSel');
      sel.innerHTML = '';
      for (const p of PRESET_LIST) {
        const opt = document.createElement('option');
        opt.value = p.id;
        opt.textContent = p.label;
        sel.appendChild(opt);
      }
      const customOpt = document.createElement('option');
      customOpt.value = 'custom';
      customOpt.textContent = 'Custom';
      sel.appendChild(customOpt);
    }

    function syncPresetSel() {
      const ids = JSON.stringify(activeTierIds);
      const m = PRESET_LIST.find(p => JSON.stringify(PRESETS[p.id]) === ids);
      document.getElementById('presetSel').value = m ? m.id : 'custom';
    }

    function autoSave() {
      try { localStorage.setItem(AUTOSAVE_KEY, JSON.stringify({ allTiers, activeTierIds, columns, tierItems, poolItems, idCounter, revivalTint, revivedSet:[...revivedSet] })); } catch(e){}
    }

    function autoLoad() {
      try {
        const raw = localStorage.getItem(AUTOSAVE_KEY); if (!raw) return false;
        const d = JSON.parse(raw);
        if (d.allTiers)      allTiers = d.allTiers;
        if (d.activeTierIds) activeTierIds = d.activeTierIds;
        if (d.columns)       { columns = d.columns; document.getElementById('colSel').value = columns; }
        if (d.tierItems)     tierItems = d.tierItems;
        if (d.poolItems)     poolItems = d.poolItems;
        if (d.idCounter)     idCounter = d.idCounter;
        if (d.revivalTint  !== undefined) { revivalTint = d.revivalTint; document.getElementById('bonusRevival').checked = revivalTint; }
        if (d.revivedSet)    revivedSet = new Set(d.revivedSet);
        syncPresetSel(); return true;
      } catch(e) { return false; }
    }

    function getSaves() { try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(SAVES_KEY) || '{}'); } catch(e) { return {}; } }

    function saveNamedList() {
      const name = document.getElementById('saveNameInput').value.trim(); if (!name) return;
      const saves = getSaves();
      saves[name] = { allTiers, activeTierIds, columns, tierItems, poolItems, idCounter, revivedSet:[...revivedSet], savedAt: Date.now() };
      try { localStorage.setItem(SAVES_KEY, JSON.stringify(saves)); } catch(e){}
      document.getElementById('saveNameInput').value = ''; renderSavesList();
    }

    function loadNamedList(name) {
      const d = getSaves()[name]; if (!d) return;
      if (d.allTiers)      allTiers = d.allTiers;
      if (d.activeTierIds) activeTierIds = d.activeTierIds;
      if (d.columns)       { columns = d.columns; document.getElementById('colSel').value = columns; }
      if (d.tierItems)     tierItems = d.tierItems;
      if (d.poolItems)     poolItems = d.poolItems;
      if (d.idCounter)     idCounter = d.idCounter;
      if (d.revivedSet)    revivedSet = new Set(d.revivedSet);
      syncPresetSel(); renderAll();
    }

    function deleteNamedList(name) {
      const saves = getSaves(); delete saves[name];
      try { localStorage.setItem(SAVES_KEY, JSON.stringify(saves)); } catch(e){} renderSavesList();
    }

    function renderSavesList() {
      const el = document.getElementById('savesList'), saves = getSaves(), keys = Object.keys(saves);
      if (!keys.length) { el.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:11px;color:hsl(var(--muted-foreground));font-style:italic;padding:4px 0">No saved lists</div>'; return; }
      el.innerHTML = '';
      keys.sort((a,b) => (saves[b].savedAt||0) - (saves[a].savedAt||0)).forEach(name => {
        const entry = document.createElement('div'); entry.className = 'save-entry';
        const nameEl = document.createElement('div'); nameEl.className = 'save-entry-name'; nameEl.textContent = name; nameEl.title = 'Click to load'; nameEl.onclick = () => loadNamedList(name);
        const del = document.createElement('button'); del.className = 'save-entry-del'; del.textContent = '✕'; del.onclick = () => deleteNamedList(name);
        entry.appendChild(nameEl); entry.appendChild(del); el.appendChild(entry);
      });
    }

    function downloadDat7(filename, content) {
      const blob = new Blob([content], { type: 'application/octet-stream' });
      const a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob); a.download = filename; a.click();
    }

    function doExport(mode) {
      let dataToExport;
      if (mode === 'full') {
        dataToExport = {
          allTiers,
          activeTierIds,
          columns,
          tierItems,
          poolItems,
          idCounter,
          revivalTint,
          revivedSet: [...revivedSet]
        };
      } else {
        dataToExport = {
          allTiers,
          activeTierIds
        };
      }
      const jsonStr = JSON.stringify(dataToExport, null, 2);
      const fname = mode === 'full' ? 'tierlist.dat7' : 'preset.dat7';
      const modal = document.getElementById('modalBox');
      modal.innerHTML = `
        <div class="modal-title">${mode === 'full' ? 'Export Tierlist' : 'Export Preset'}</div>
        <div class="modal-row" style="font-size:11px;color:hsl(var(--muted-foreground))">Your ${fname} is ready to download, or copy the code below.</div>
        <div class="modal-row"><label>Code</label><textarea id="b64out" readonly onclick="this.select()" style="font-size:9px;word-break:break-all">${escHtml(jsonStr)}</textarea></div>
        <div class="b64-copy-row">
          <button class="btn-primary" onclick="downloadDat7('${fname}', document.getElementById('b64out').value)">Download ${fname}</button>
          <button onclick="navigator.clipboard.writeText(document.getElementById('b64out').value).then(()=>{this.textContent='Copied!';setTimeout(()=>this.textContent='Copy Code',1500)})">Copy Code</button>
          <button onclick="closeModal()">Close</button>
        </div>`;
      openModal();
    }

    function doImport(mode) {
      const modal = document.getElementById('modalBox');
      modal.innerHTML = `
        <div class="modal-title">${mode === 'full' ? 'Import Tierlist' : 'Import Preset'}</div>
        <div class="modal-row"><label>Upload .dat7 file</label>
          <input type="file" id="dat7file" accept=".dat7" style="width:100%;background:transparent;border:none;padding:0;color:hsl(var(--foreground));font-size:11px">
        </div>
        <div class="modal-row"><label>Or paste code</label><textarea id="b64in" placeholder="Paste exported JSON code..."></textarea></div>
        <div class="modal-btns">
          <button onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>
          <button class="btn-primary" onclick="applyImport('${mode}')">Import</button>
        </div>`;
      document.getElementById('dat7file').addEventListener('change', function() {
        const file = this.files[0]; if (!file) return;
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = ev => { document.getElementById('b64in').value = ev.target.result; };
        reader.readAsText(file);
      });
      openModal();
    }

    function applyImport(mode) {
      try {
        const raw = document.getElementById('b64in').value.trim();
        const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
        if (parsed.allTiers) allTiers = parsed.allTiers;
        if (parsed.activeTierIds) activeTierIds = parsed.activeTierIds;
        if (mode === 'full') {
          columns = parsed.columns || 1;
          tierItems = parsed.tierItems || {};
          poolItems = parsed.poolItems || [];
          idCounter = parsed.idCounter || 0;
          revivalTint = parsed.revivalTint || false;
          revivedSet = new Set(parsed.revivedSet || []);
          document.getElementById('colSel').value = columns;
          document.getElementById('bonusRevival').checked = revivalTint;
        }
        closeModal();
        syncPresetSel();
        renderAll();
      } catch(e) { 
        alert('Invalid JSON. Make sure you pasted the exact exported code.'); 
      }
    }

    function renderAll() {
      document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--tier-cols', columns);
      document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--tier-rows', String(Math.ceil(activeTierIds.length / columns)));
      renderTiers(); renderPool(); autoSave();
    }

    function renderTiers() {
      const list = document.getElementById('tierList'); list.innerHTML = '';
      getActiveTiers().forEach(tier => {
        const row = document.createElement('div');
        row.className = 'tier-row' + (tier.isExec ? ' is-exec-row' : '');
        row.dataset.tierId = tier.id;

        const lbl = document.createElement('div');
        lbl.className = 'tier-label' + (tier.label.length > 4 ? ' long-label' : '');
        lbl.style.background = tier.color; lbl.style.color = tier.text;
        const lblText = document.createElement('span'); lblText.textContent = tier.label; lbl.appendChild(lblText);
        const lblBtns = document.createElement('div'); lblBtns.className = 'tier-label-btns';
        const editBtn = document.createElement('button'); editBtn.className = 'tier-lbl-btn'; editBtn.textContent = '✎';
        editBtn.onclick = e => { e.stopPropagation(); openEditTier(tier.id); };
        lblBtns.appendChild(editBtn); lbl.appendChild(lblBtns); row.appendChild(lbl);

        const itemsDiv = document.createElement('div');
        itemsDiv.className = 'tier-items';
        itemsDiv.dataset.tier = tier.id;
        setupDrop(itemsDiv);
        const tierItemList = tierItems[tier.id] || [];
        const MAX_PER_ROW = 5;
        if (tierItemList.length === 0) {
          const emptyRow = document.createElement('div');
          emptyRow.className = 'tier-item-row';
          itemsDiv.appendChild(emptyRow);
        } else {
          const chunks = [];
          for (let i = 0; i < tierItemList.length; i += MAX_PER_ROW) chunks.push(tierItemList.slice(i, i + MAX_PER_ROW));
          chunks.forEach(chunk => {
            const rowDiv = document.createElement('div');
            rowDiv.className = 'tier-item-row';
            chunk.forEach(item => rowDiv.appendChild(makeTiltWrapper(item, tier.id)));
            itemsDiv.appendChild(rowDiv);
          });
        }
        row.appendChild(itemsDiv);
        list.appendChild(row);
      });
    }

    function renderPool() {
      const pool = document.getElementById('pool'); pool.innerHTML = '';
      if (!poolItems.length) {
        const emp = document.createElement('div'); emp.className = 'pool-empty'; emp.textContent = 'add items below'; pool.appendChild(emp); return;
      }
      poolItems.forEach(item => pool.appendChild(makeTiltWrapper(item, '__pool__')));
      setupDrop(pool);
    }

    function handleTilt(e, wrapper) {
      const card = wrapper.querySelector('.tl-item');
      const rect = wrapper.getBoundingClientRect();
      const clientX = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
      const clientY = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;
      const x = clientX - rect.left, y = clientY - rect.top;
      const cx = rect.width / 2, cy = rect.height / 2;
      card.style.transform = 'rotateX(' + ((cy-y)/6) + 'deg) rotateY(' + ((x-cx)/10) + 'deg) scale3d(1.06,1.06,1.06)';
    }

    function makeTiltWrapper(item, tier) {
      const wrap = document.createElement('div'); wrap.className = 'tilt-wrapper';
      wrap.dataset.itemId = item.id; wrap.dataset.fromTier = tier; wrap.draggable = true;
      const card = makeItemCard(item, tier); wrap.appendChild(card);
      wrap.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => wrap.classList.add('is-tapped'));
      wrap.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => { wrap.classList.remove('is-tapped'); card.style.transform = 'rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) scale3d(1,1,1)'; });
      wrap.addEventListener('mousemove', e => handleTilt(e, wrap));
      wrap.addEventListener('touchstart', e => {
        document.querySelectorAll('.tilt-wrapper.is-tapped').forEach(w => { w.classList.remove('is-tapped'); const c = w.querySelector('.tl-item'); if (c) c.style.transform = 'rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) scale3d(1,1,1)'; });
        wrap.classList.add('is-tapped'); handleTilt(e, wrap);
      }, { passive: true });
      wrap.addEventListener('touchmove', e => handleTilt(e, wrap), { passive: true });
      wrap.addEventListener('touchend', () => { wrap.classList.remove('is-tapped'); card.style.transform = 'rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) scale3d(1,1,1)'; });
      wrap.addEventListener('dragstart', e => { dragItem = item; dragSrc = tier; setTimeout(() => wrap.style.opacity = '0.3', 0); e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move'; });
      wrap.addEventListener('dragend', () => { wrap.style.opacity = ''; });
      return wrap;
    }

    function makeItemCard(item, tier) {
      const card = document.createElement('div');
      const isRevived = revivalTint && revivedSet.has(item.id) && tier !== '__pool__' && !isExecTier(tier);
      card.className = 'tl-item' + (isRevived ? ' revived' : '');

      if (item.type === 'image') {
        card.style.padding = '0'; card.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        if (item.url) {
          const img = document.createElement('img'); img.className = 'tl-item-img-full'; img.src = item.url;
          img.onerror = () => { img.style.display = 'none'; };
          card.appendChild(img);
        }
        if (item.label && item.label !== item.url) {
          const lbl = document.createElement('div'); lbl.className = 'tl-item-img-label'; lbl.textContent = item.label;
          card.appendChild(lbl);
        }
      } else {
        if (item.type === 'spotify' || item.type === 'ytmusic' || item.type === 'video') {
          const ic = document.createElement('div');
          if (item.type === 'spotify') { ic.className = 'tl-item-icon icon-spotify'; ic.textContent = '♫'; }
          else if (item.type === 'ytmusic') { ic.className = 'tl-item-icon icon-yt'; ic.textContent = '▶'; }
          else { ic.className = 'tl-item-icon icon-video'; ic.textContent = '▶'; }
          card.appendChild(ic);
        }
        const block = document.createElement('div'); block.className = 'tl-item-text-block';
        const lbl = document.createElement('div'); lbl.className = 'tl-item-label'; lbl.textContent = item.label;
        if (item.url) { lbl.style.cursor = 'pointer'; lbl.onclick = e => { e.stopPropagation(); window.open(item.url, '_blank'); }; }
        block.appendChild(lbl);
        if (item.type !== 'text') {
          const tp = document.createElement('div'); tp.className = 'tl-item-type'; tp.textContent = item.type; block.appendChild(tp);
        }
        card.appendChild(block);
      }

      const editBtn = document.createElement('button'); editBtn.className = 'tl-item-edit'; editBtn.textContent = '✎';
      editBtn.onclick = e => { e.stopPropagation(); openEditItem(item, tier); }; card.appendChild(editBtn);
      const rem = document.createElement('button'); rem.className = 'tl-item-remove'; rem.textContent = '✕';
      rem.onclick = e => { e.stopPropagation(); removeItem(item.id, tier); }; card.appendChild(rem);
      return card;
    }

    function setupDrop(el) {
      el.addEventListener('dragover', e => { e.preventDefault(); el.classList.add('drag-over'); });
      el.addEventListener('dragleave', e => { if (!el.contains(e.relatedTarget)) el.classList.remove('drag-over'); });
      el.addEventListener('drop', e => {
        e.preventDefault(); el.classList.remove('drag-over'); if (!dragItem) return;
        const dest = el.dataset.tier;
        if (dest === dragSrc) { dragItem = null; dragSrc = null; return; }
        if (revivalTint && isExecTier(dest)) revivedSet.add(dragItem.id);
        removeFromSrc(dragItem.id, dragSrc);
        if (dest === '__pool__') poolItems.push(dragItem);
        else { if (!tierItems[dest]) tierItems[dest] = []; tierItems[dest].push(dragItem); }
        dragItem = null; dragSrc = null; renderAll();
      });
    }
    function removeItem(id, tier) {
      if (tier === '__pool__') poolItems = poolItems.filter(i => i.id !== id);
      else tierItems[tier] = (tierItems[tier] || []).filter(i => i.id !== id);
      renderAll();
    }
    function removeFromSrc(id, tier) {
      if (tier === '__pool__') poolItems = poolItems.filter(i => i.id !== id);
      else tierItems[tier] = (tierItems[tier] || []).filter(i => i.id !== id);
    }
    function findItem(id) {
      for (const item of poolItems) if (item.id === id) return item;
      for (const arr of Object.values(tierItems)) for (const item of arr) if (item.id === id) return item;
      return null;
    }

    function addItem(overrides = {}) {
      const type    = overrides.type  ?? document.getElementById('itemType').value;
      const input   = overrides.input !== undefined ? overrides.input : document.getElementById('itemInput').value.trim();
      const labelIn = overrides.label !== undefined ? overrides.label : document.getElementById('itemLabel').value.trim();
      if (!input && !overrides.dataUrl) return;
      const item = { id: 'item_' + (++idCounter), type, url: null, label: '' };
      if (overrides.dataUrl) { item.type = 'image'; item.url = overrides.dataUrl; item.label = ''; }
      else if (type === 'text') { item.label = input; item.url = null; }
      else { item.url = input; item.label = labelIn; }
      poolItems.push(item);
      if (!overrides.dataUrl) { document.getElementById('itemInput').value = ''; document.getElementById('itemLabel').value = ''; }
      renderAll();
    }

    function openEditItem(item, tier) {
      const showRevive = revivalTint && revivedSet.has(item.id);
      const modal = document.getElementById('modalBox');
      modal.innerHTML = `
        <div class="modal-title">Edit Item</div>
        <div class="modal-row"><label>Label</label><input type="text" id="ei-label" value="${escHtml(item.label)}"></div>
        <div class="modal-row"><label>URL (optional)</label><input type="text" id="ei-url" value="${escHtml(item.url||'')}"></div>
        ${showRevive ? `<div class="modal-check-row"><input type="checkbox" id="ei-clearrevive"><label for="ei-clearrevive">Clear revival tint</label></div>` : ''}
        <div class="modal-btns">
          <button onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>
          <button class="btn-primary" onclick="saveEditItem('${item.id}')">Save</button>
        </div>`;
      openModal();
    }
    function saveEditItem(id) {
      const item = findItem(id); if (!item) { closeModal(); return; }
      const lv = document.getElementById('ei-label').value.trim(); if (lv) item.label = lv;
      const uv = document.getElementById('ei-url'); if (uv) item.url = uv.value.trim() || null;
      const cv = document.getElementById('ei-clearrevive'); if (cv && cv.checked) revivedSet.delete(id);
      closeModal(); renderAll();
    }

    function openEditTier(id) {
      const tier = getTier(id); if (!tier) return;
      const modal = document.getElementById('modalBox');
      modal.innerHTML = `
        <div class="modal-title">Edit Tier</div>
        <div class="modal-row"><label>Label</label><input type="text" id="et-label" value="${escHtml(tier.label)}" maxlength="12"></div>
        <div class="modal-row">
          <label>Color</label>
          <div class="modal-color-row" id="et-presets">
            ${PRESET_COLORS.map(c => `<div class="color-preset${tier.color===c?' active':''}" style="background:${c}" data-c="${c}" onclick="pickPresetColor('${c}')"></div>`).join('')}
            <input type="color" id="et-color" value="${tier.color}">
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="modal-row"><label>Tint Color</label><input type="color" id="et-text" value="${tier.text.startsWith('#') ? tier.text : '#ffffff'}"></div>
        <div class="modal-check-row">
          <input type="checkbox" id="et-exec" ${tier.isExec ? 'checked' : ''}>
          <label for="et-exec">Execution Rank</label>
        </div>
        <div class="modal-btns">
          <button onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button>
          <button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="deleteTier('${id}')">Delete</button>
          <button class="btn-primary" onclick="saveEditTier('${id}')">Save</button>
        </div>`;
      document.getElementById('et-color').addEventListener('input', () => document.querySelectorAll('#et-presets .color-preset').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active')));
      openModal();
    }
    function pickPresetColor(c) {
      document.getElementById('et-color').value = c;
      document.querySelectorAll('#et-presets .color-preset').forEach(el => el.classList.toggle('active', el.dataset.c === c));
    }
    function saveEditTier(id) {
      const tier = getTier(id); if (!tier) { closeModal(); return; }
      tier.label  = document.getElementById('et-label').value.trim() || tier.label;
      tier.color  = document.getElementById('et-color').value;
      tier.text   = document.getElementById('et-text').value;
      tier.isExec = document.getElementById('et-exec').checked;
      closeModal(); syncPresetSel(); renderAll();
    }
    function deleteTier(id) {
      allTiers = allTiers.filter(t => t.id !== id);
      activeTierIds = activeTierIds.filter(i => i !== id);
      poolItems.push(...(tierItems[id] || []));
      delete tierItems[id];
      closeModal(); syncPresetSel(); renderAll();
    }

    function openManageTiers() {
      const modal = document.getElementById('modalBox'); modal.innerHTML = '';
      const title = document.createElement('div'); title.className = 'modal-title'; title.textContent = 'Manage Tiers'; modal.appendChild(title);
      const list = document.createElement('div'); list.className = 'tier-manage-list';
      function rebuildList() {
        list.innerHTML = '';
        getActiveTiers().forEach((tier, idx) => {
          const entry = document.createElement('div'); entry.className = 'tier-manage-entry';
          const swatch = document.createElement('div'); swatch.className = 'swatch'; swatch.style.background = tier.color;
          const lbl = document.createElement('div'); lbl.className = 'lbl'; lbl.textContent = tier.label;
          const btns = document.createElement('div'); btns.className = 'tier-manage-btns';
          if (tier.isExec) { const badge = document.createElement('span'); badge.className = 'exec-badge'; badge.textContent = 'EXEC'; btns.appendChild(badge); }
          const upBtn = document.createElement('button'); upBtn.className = 'btn-sm'; upBtn.textContent = '↑';
          upBtn.onclick = () => { if (idx > 0) { [activeTierIds[idx-1], activeTierIds[idx]] = [activeTierIds[idx], activeTierIds[idx-1]]; rebuildList(); } };
          const dnBtn = document.createElement('button'); dnBtn.className = 'btn-sm'; dnBtn.textContent = '↓';
          dnBtn.onclick = () => { if (idx < activeTierIds.length-1) { [activeTierIds[idx], activeTierIds[idx+1]] = [activeTierIds[idx+1], activeTierIds[idx]]; rebuildList(); } };
          const edBtn = document.createElement('button'); edBtn.className = 'btn-sm'; edBtn.textContent = '✎';
          edBtn.onclick = () => { closeModal(); openEditTier(tier.id); };
          btns.appendChild(upBtn); btns.appendChild(dnBtn); btns.appendChild(edBtn);
          entry.appendChild(swatch); entry.appendChild(lbl); entry.appendChild(btns); list.appendChild(entry);
        });
      }
      rebuildList(); modal.appendChild(list);
      const addTitle = document.createElement('div');
      addTitle.style.cssText = 'font-size:10px;color:hsl(var(--muted-foreground));text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;padding-top:8px;border-top:1px solid hsl(var(--border))';
      addTitle.textContent = 'Add New Tier'; modal.appendChild(addTitle);
      const newRow = document.createElement('div'); newRow.style.cssText = 'display:flex;gap:6px;align-items:center;flex-wrap:wrap';
      const newLabel = document.createElement('input'); newLabel.type = 'text'; newLabel.id = 'tm-newlabel'; newLabel.placeholder = 'Label'; newLabel.style.cssText = 'flex:1;min-width:60px';
      const newColor = document.createElement('input'); newColor.type = 'color'; newColor.id = 'tm-newcolor'; newColor.value = '#888888';
      const newExecWrap = document.createElement('label'); newExecWrap.style.cssText = 'display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;font-size:11px;cursor:pointer';
      const newExecCb = document.createElement('input'); newExecCb.type = 'checkbox'; newExecCb.id = 'tm-newexec';
      newExecWrap.appendChild(newExecCb); newExecWrap.appendChild(document.createTextNode('Exec'));
      const addBtn = document.createElement('button'); addBtn.className = 'btn-primary btn-sm'; addBtn.textContent = '+ Add';
      addBtn.onclick = () => {
        const lbl = document.getElementById('tm-newlabel').value.trim(); if (!lbl) return;
        const color = document.getElementById('tm-newcolor').value;
        const isExec = document.getElementById('tm-newexec').checked;
        const brightness = parseInt(color.slice(1,3),16)*0.299 + parseInt(color.slice(3,5),16)*0.587 + parseInt(color.slice(5,7),16)*0.114;
        const text = brightness > 128 ? '#1a1a1a' : '#ffffff';
        const newId = 'custom_' + Date.now();
        allTiers.push({ id: newId, label: lbl, color, text, isExec });
        activeTierIds.push(newId);
        document.getElementById('tm-newlabel').value = ''; rebuildList();
      };
      newRow.appendChild(newLabel); newRow.appendChild(newColor); newRow.appendChild(newExecWrap); newRow.appendChild(addBtn); modal.appendChild(newRow);
      const btns = document.createElement('div'); btns.className = 'modal-btns';
      const doneBtn = document.createElement('button'); doneBtn.className = 'btn-primary'; doneBtn.textContent = 'Done';
      doneBtn.onclick = () => { closeModal(); syncPresetSel(); renderAll(); };
      btns.appendChild(doneBtn); modal.appendChild(btns);
      openModal();
    }

    function openModal()  { document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.add('open'); }
    function closeModal() { document.getElementById('modalOverlay').classList.remove('open'); }
    document.getElementById('modalOverlay').addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === document.getElementById('modalOverlay')) closeModal(); });
    function escHtml(s) { return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;'); }

    function saveImage() {
      const s = document.createElement('script'); s.src = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/html2canvas/1.4.1/html2canvas.min.js';
      s.onload = () => { html2canvas(document.getElementById('tierList'), { backgroundColor: '#1a1a1a', scale: 2, useCORS: true }).then(canvas => { const a = document.createElement('a'); a.download = 'tierlist.png'; a.href = canvas.toDataURL('image/png'); a.click(); }); };
      document.head.appendChild(s);
    }

    document.getElementById('itemType').addEventListener('change', function() {
      document.getElementById('itemLabel').style.display = (this.value !== 'text' && this.value !== 'image') ? 'block' : 'none';
      document.getElementById('itemInput').placeholder = this.value === 'text' ? 'Label...' : 'Paste URL...';
    });
    document.getElementById('itemInput').addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') addItem(); });
    document.getElementById('presetSel').addEventListener('change', function() {
      const v = this.value; if (v === 'custom') return;
      if (!PRESETS[v]) return;
      allTiers = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(TIERS_BASE)); activeTierIds = [...PRESETS[v]]; renderAll();
    });
    document.getElementById('colSel').addEventListener('change', function() { columns = parseInt(this.value); renderAll(); });
    document.getElementById('bonusRevival').addEventListener('change', function() { revivalTint = this.checked; renderAll(); });

    document.addEventListener('paste', e => {
      const items = e.clipboardData?.items;
      if (!items) return;
      for (const item of items) {
        if (item.type.startsWith('image/')) {
          const file = item.getAsFile();
          const reader = new FileReader();
          reader.onload = ev => addItem({ dataUrl: ev.target.result });
          reader.readAsDataURL(file);
          return;
        }
      }
      const text = e.clipboardData.getData('text/plain').trim();
      if (!text) return;
      const active = document.activeElement;
      if (active && (active.tagName === 'INPUT' || active.tagName === 'TEXTAREA')) return;
      const isUrl = /^https?:\/\//.test(text);
      if (isUrl) {
        const isImg = /\.(jpg|jpeg|png|gif|webp|svg|avif)(\?|$)/i.test(text);
        addItem({ type: isImg ? 'image' : 'text', input: text, label: '' });
      } else {
        addItem({ type: 'text', input: text, label: '' });
      }
    });

    document.addEventListener('touchstart', e => {
      if (!e.target.closest('.tilt-wrapper')) document.querySelectorAll('.tilt-wrapper.is-tapped').forEach(w => { w.classList.remove('is-tapped'); const c = w.querySelector('.tl-item'); if (c) c.style.transform = 'rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) scale3d(1,1,1)'; });
    }, { passive: true });

    document.getElementById('pool').dataset.tier = '__pool__';
    setupDrop(document.getElementById('pool'));

    loadRankingDat().then(() => {
      const loaded = autoLoad();
      if (!loaded) poolItems = [{ id: 'item_' + idCounter++, type: 'text', label: 'drag me to a tier', url: null }];
      renderAll();
      renderSavesList();
    });
  </script>
  </body>
</html>

    <script>
        const DateTime = luxon.DateTime;

        const TZ_ABBREVIATIONS = {
            'AST': 'America/Halifax',
            'ADT': 'America/Halifax',
            'EST': 'America/New_York', 
            'EDT': 'America/New_York',
            'CST': 'America/Chicago', 
            'CDT': 'America/Chicago',
            'MST': 'America/Denver', 
            'MDT': 'America/Denver',
            'PST': 'America/Los_Angeles', 
            'PDT': 'America/Los_Angeles',
            'AEST': 'Australia/Sydney', 
            'AEDT': 'Australia/Sydney',
            'BST': 'Europe/London', 
            'IST': 'Asia/Kolkata',
            'JST': 'Asia/Tokyo', 
            'KST': 'Asia/Seoul',
            'CET': 'Europe/Paris', 
            'CEST': 'Europe/Paris',
            'HKT': 'Asia/Hong_Kong', 
            'SGT': 'Asia/Singapore',
            'HST': 'Pacific/Honolulu', 
            'AKST': 'America/Anchorage',
            'WET': 'Europe/Lisbon',
            'MSK': 'Europe/Moscow'
        };

        let clocks = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('world-clocks')) || ['local', 'UTC', 'America/New_York', 'Asia/Tokyo'];
        let is24Hour = localStorage.getItem('clock-format') !== '12h';

        // Populate Datalist with all valid IANA zones
        const datalist = document.getElementById('tz-list');
        Intl.supportedValuesOf('timeZone').forEach(tz => {
            const opt = document.createElement('option');
            opt.value = tz;
            datalist.appendChild(opt);
        });

        function toggleFormat() {
            is24Hour = !is24Hour;
            localStorage.setItem('clock-format', is24Hour ? '24h' : '12h');
            updateDisplay();
        }

        function addClock() {
            clocks.push('UTC');
            save();
            render();
        }

        function removeClock(index) {
            clocks.splice(index, 1);
            save();
            render();
        }

        function updateClockTimezone(index, val) {
            clocks[index] = val;
            save();
            updateDisplay();
        }

        function save() {
            localStorage.setItem('world-clocks', JSON.stringify(clocks));
        }

        /**
         * Resolves a string input to a Luxon DateTime object
         */
        function getLuxonTime(input) {
            const cleanInput = input.trim();
            const upperInput = cleanInput.toUpperCase();
            
            // 1. Check for 'local' keyword
            if (upperInput === 'LOCAL') return DateTime.now();

            // 2. Check manual abbreviation map
            if (TZ_ABBREVIATIONS[upperInput]) {
                return DateTime.now().setZone(TZ_ABBREVIATIONS[upperInput]);
            }

            // 3. Check for Offset (e.g., UTC+5, -8, +05:30)
            const offsetMatch = cleanInput.match(/^(?:UTC|GMT)?([+-]\d{1,2}:?\d{0,2})$/i);
            if (offsetMatch) {
                return DateTime.now().setZone(`UTC${offsetMatch[1]}`);
            }

            // 4. Try as IANA name (e.g., Africa/Cairo)
            const dt = DateTime.now().setZone(cleanInput);
            if (dt.isValid) return dt;

            return null;
        }

        function getOffsetInfo(input) {
            const target = getLuxonTime(input);
            if (!target || !target.isValid) {
                return { timeStr: "Invalid TZ", utcText: "---", diffText: "---", label: "Unknown" };
            }

            const local = DateTime.now();
            
            // Format time
            const timeStr = target.toFormat(is24Hour ? 'HH:mm:ss' : 'hh:mm:ss a');
            
            // Get Offset from UTC (e.g., UTC +5.5)
            const offsetHours = target.offset / 60;
            const utcText = `UTC ${offsetHours >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${offsetHours}`;

            // Calculate Difference from local system time
            const diffInHours = (target.offset - local.offset) / 60;
            let diffText = "";
            if (diffInHours === 0) {
                diffText = "Same as local";
            } else {
                const absDiff = Math.abs(diffInHours);
                diffText = `${absDiff}h ${diffInHours > 0 ? 'ahead of' : 'behind'} local`;
            }

            return { 
                timeStr, 
                utcText, 
                diffText, 
                label: target.zoneName === 'local' ? 'Local System' : target.offsetNameLong 
            };
        }

        function render() {
            const container = document.getElementById('clocks-container');
            document.getElementById('format-toggle').textContent = is24Hour ? '24H' : '12H';
            
            container.innerHTML = clocks.map((currentTz, index) => `
                <div class="card">
                    <div class="card-header">
                        <input type="text" 
                               class="tz-input" 
                               list="tz-list" 
                               value="${currentTz}" 
                               placeholder="Enter Zone (e.g. PST, UTC+7, Europe/London)"
                               oninput="updateClockTimezone(${index}, this.value)">
                        <button class="btn-remove" onclick="removeClock(${index})">✕</button>
                    </div>
                    <div class="time-display" id="time-${index}">--:--:--</div>
                    <div class="stats-row">
                        <span>Zone: <b id="label-${index}">---</b></span>
                        <span>Offset: <b id="utc-${index}">---</b></span>
                        <span>Relative: <b id="diff-${index}">---</b></span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            updateDisplay();
        }

        function updateDisplay() {
            clocks.forEach((tz, index) => {
                const data = getOffsetInfo(tz);
                const t = document.getElementById(`time-${index}`);
                const u = document.getElementById(`utc-${index}`);
                const d = document.getElementById(`diff-${index}`);
                const l = document.getElementById(`label-${index}`);
                
                if (t) t.textContent = data.timeStr;
                if (u) u.textContent = data.utcText;
                if (d) d.textContent = data.diffText;
                if (l) l.textContent = data.label;
            });
        }

        setInterval(updateDisplay, 1000);
        render();

    </script>
</body>
</html>

(CONTENT END)

File: storage/internal/pages/custom/writing/books/hs/omom/chapter_1.md

(CONTENT START)

The screech of tires was the first sound, a violent tearing of rubber against asphalt that etched itself into the boy's memory. Then came the sickening crunch of metal, a percussive, final sound like the world snapping a bone. He hadn't seen it, not with his own eyes. He, his older sister, and even older brother were waiting on the porch, a melting carton of ice cream sweating between them, the sweet scent of vanilla a cloying perfume in the humid afternoon air. They were waiting for their mother to pull into the driveway, to emerge from the car with her weary but ever-present smile. She never did.

The silence that followed the crash was a living thing, a heavy blanket that smothered the cheerful birdsong and the distant hum of lawnmowers. It was his sister who broke it, her voice a thin, reedy thing that trembled with a question they all felt but dared not ask. His brother, ever the stoic one, was already moving, his lanky frame vaulting over the porch railing and sprinting towards the intersection at the end of their street. The boy remained frozen, the carton of ice cream now a puddle at his feet, the sweet smell turning sour in his nostrils.

What he saw when he finally forced his legs to move was a tableau of such brutal finality that his mind refused to process it. The family car, their mother's car, was a mangled accordion of steel and shattered glass, wrapped around a thick oak tree with an intimacy that was obscene. A single, slender arm, limp and unnaturally pale, dangled from the driver's side window, a silent, beckoning gesture. He remembered the paramedics, their faces grim and set, the practiced, almost bored way they moved. He remembered the crimson that stained the pristine white of the airbag, a grotesque parody of a blossoming flower. He remembered the sheet, the stark, impersonal white of it as it was draped over what was once his mother.

His siblings wept. His sister's cries were ragged, gasping sobs that tore at her throat. His brother's tears were silent, carving clean paths through the grime on his face as he stood, a silent, shaking sentinel. But the boy did not cry. A cold, hard knot had formed in his stomach, a core of ice that spread through his veins, numbing him to the grief that swirled around him like a suffocating fog. This couldn't be it. It was too sudden, too mundane, too… wrong. A life as vibrant as his mother's couldn't simply be extinguished by a moment of inattention, a slick patch of road. It was an unacceptable equation, a cosmic error that he, and only he, seemed to recognize.

In the days that followed, a suffocating quiet descended upon their house. The sympathy cards piled up on the mantelpiece, their platitudes and condolences feeling like insults. His siblings moved through the house like ghosts, their faces etched with a shared, hollowed-out sorrow. They spoke in whispers, their conversations punctuated by long, aching silences. They were giving up. He could see it in their eyes, in the way they'd started to pack away her things, to erase her presence from the very air they breathed. They were accepting the unacceptable.

He couldn't. He wouldn't. The thought, at first a flicker in the back of his mind, began to grow, to take root, to blossom into a terrible and beautiful idea. They had given up on her, but he would not. He would bring her back. He had to.

His obsession began in the sterile silence of the local library, poring over arcane medical texts and dusty anatomical charts. He devoured information on neurology, on cellular regeneration, on the very essence of what constituted life. He learned about the brain, that delicate, intricate organ that housed the soul, the memories, the very being of a person. That was the key. Her body was broken, shattered beyond repair, but her mind, her essence… that could be saved.

The plan, when it finally coalesced in his mind, was both monstrous and breathtakingly simple. He would retrieve her brain, the vessel of her soul. He would repair her body, piece by piece. And then, he would return her to them. He would make them see. He would make them understand.

The morgue was a place of cold, clinical indifference. The air was thick with the scent of disinfectant and something else, something cloying and sweet that hinted at the decay it was meant to mask. He'd snuck in through a loading bay, his heart a frantic drum against his ribs. He found her in a refrigerated drawer, a tag on her toe bearing her name, a name that felt alien and distant now. She was a specimen, a piece of meat waiting to be processed.

Seeing her like that, her body a patchwork of crude stitches and angry bruises, only strengthened his resolve. This was not his mother. This was a broken vessel, a ruined temple. But the divine spark, the thing that made her *her*, was still salvageable.

He'd come prepared. A small, insulated cooler, a set of surgical tools he'd painstakingly acquired, and a diagram of the human skull he'd memorized until he could trace its every suture in his sleep. The act itself was a blur of focused, almost reverent, butchery. The sound of the bone saw was a high, keening whine that echoed in the sterile silence. The feel of the brain, a delicate, yielding mass in his hands, was both horrifying and exhilarating. He placed it carefully in the cooler, nestled amongst bags of ice, a precious, irreplaceable treasure.

Back in the relative sanctuary of his basement, he began his work. He'd cleared a corner, setting up a makeshift laboratory with a cold, methodical precision. He'd started with animals. A stray cat, its body still warm, its death a small, insignificant tragedy in the grand scheme of things. He'd practiced his stitches, his sutures, his clumsy attempts at taxidermy. His hands, once clumsy and hesitant, became steady, sure. He learned the give and pull of sinew and muscle, the delicate architecture of bone.

His siblings, wrapped in their own cocoons of grief, barely noticed his increasingly erratic behavior. They saw his late nights in the basement as a way of coping, a distraction from the gaping wound their mother's death had left in their lives. They didn't see the glint in his eye, the feverish intensity with which he worked. They didn't smell the faint, metallic tang of blood that clung to his clothes, a scent he'd become so accustomed to he no longer noticed it.

His mother's body, retrieved in a second, more audacious, trip to the mortuary, now lay on a makeshift operating table in the center of his subterranean sanctuary. The damage was extensive, a brutal roadmap of her final moments. But he was not deterred. He would fix her. He would make her whole again.

He worked tirelessly, fueled by a potent cocktail of grief, madness, and a terrifyingly unwavering love. He scavenged for parts, for pieces to replace what was lost. The neighborhood pets began to disappear, their small, furry bodies offered up to his gruesome cause. He became a silent, nocturnal predator, his grief twisting him into something monstrous.

And all the while, he talked to her. He would sit for hours by the cooler where her brain rested in its icy bath, whispering to her, telling her of his progress, of his unwavering devotion. He would tell her how her other children had abandoned her, how they had accepted her death with a passivity that bordered on betrayal. But not him. He was her faithful son, her little lamb. And he would not fail her. He would bring her back from the silent, unforgiving dark. He would make her whole again, no matter the cost. The scent of formaldehyde and something far more sinister began to permeate the basement, a testament to his unholy work, a harbinger of the horrors yet to come.

(CONTENT END)

The basement had transformed. What was once a dusty repository of forgotten furniture and childhood relics was now a charnel house, a grotesque cathedral dedicated to a singular, blasphemous purpose. The air was thick and heavy, a sickly sweet miasma of formaldehyde, stale blood, and the cloying perfume of decaying flesh that clung to the back of the throat and infiltrated every breath. At the center of this profane stage, beneath the stark, unforgiving glare of a single bare bulb, lay the object of the boy's obsession.

His mother. Or rather, the thing he was sculpting from the wreckage of her former self. Her body, once a roadmap of catastrophic injuries, was now a horrifying mosaic of mismatched parts. The skin of a stray dog, crudely stitched and stretched to cover a gaping wound in her thigh, its fur a bizarre and unsettling patch against her pale flesh. The leg of a deer, procured from the side of the highway, grafted onto her shattered hip, the delicate hoof a grotesque parody of a human foot. He worked with the focused intensity of a master craftsman, his hands, once hesitant, now moving with a chilling, practiced grace. He was no longer just repairing; he was improving, perfecting, creating a vessel worthy of her return.

His conversations with the brain had become more frequent, more… real. In the echoing silence of the basement, he would press his ear to the cold, sterile surface of the cooler, and he would hear her. Her voice, a faint, ethereal whisper that seemed to emanate from the very depths of his own mind, would offer words of encouragement, of love, of pride. *You're doing so well, my sweet boy. You're my faithful lamb. They don't understand, but I do. I always have.*

His siblings' concern had begun to curdle into a gnawing fear. The whispers in the hallways had ceased, replaced by a tense, heavy silence. They no longer asked what he was doing in the basement. They no longer tried to coax him out for meals. They had started to lock their bedroom doors at night.

His sister was the first to breach his subterranean sanctuary. She had come down under the pretense of looking for an old photo album, her voice a thin, wavering thread in the oppressive darkness. The sight that greeted her, the monstrous effigy on the table, the array of bloodstained tools, the overpowering stench of death, had stolen the breath from her lungs. Her scream was a raw, primal sound of pure, unadulterated terror.

He had been gentle with her, at first. He had tried to explain, to make her see the beauty in his creation, the love that fueled his gruesome work. He had shown her the brain, nestled in its icy cradle, had told her of their mother's whispers, of her imminent return. But she had looked at him with eyes wide with horror and revulsion, as if he were a monster, a stranger.

*You're insane,* she had whispered, her voice trembling, her face a mask of disbelief. *This… this is a desecration. Mom is gone. You have to let her go.*

Her words were like a physical blow, a betrayal that cut deeper than any knife. She didn't understand. She couldn't. She was one of *them*, the ones who had given up, the ones who had accepted the unacceptable. A cold, chilling calm had settled over him. He had realized then that she was an obstacle, a doubter who could not be allowed to interfere. He had locked her in her room, the click of the lock a final, definitive sound. She was a lamb that had strayed from the flock, and the shepherd had to bring her back into the fold.

His brother was a different matter. He was stronger, more resolute. He had come to the basement not with fear, but with a cold, simmering rage. He had seen the truth in his sister's frantic, terrified whispers. The confrontation was inevitable, a storm that had been brewing in the strained silence of their home.

He burst into the basement, his face a thunderous mask of fury. "What have you done?" he had roared, his voice echoing off the damp concrete walls. He had seen the abomination on the table, the macabre tapestry of flesh and bone, and a guttural cry of rage and grief had been ripped from his throat.

They fought. It was a brutal, clumsy affair, a desperate struggle amidst the tools of the boy's unholy trade. His brother, fueled by righteous fury, was stronger, but the boy, in his madness, was relentless. He fought with the ferocity of a cornered animal, his movements fueled by a singular, unwavering purpose. He saw not his brother, but an impediment, a threat to his sacred mission.

In the end, it was a scalpel that decided the outcome. A small, precise instrument that he had used to carve and shape his mother's new form. He plunged it into his brother's side, the blade sinking into flesh with a sickening, wet sound. His brother's eyes had widened in shock, in a dawning, horrified understanding. He had stumbled back, a hand pressed to the wound, his face a canvas of pain and betrayal.

"Why?" he had gasped, his voice a choked, gurgling whisper.

*For her,* the boy had thought, the words a silent, fervent prayer. *For our mother. **My** mother.*

He had not felt remorse, not then. Only a cold, clear sense of purpose. His brother was another sacrifice, another offering on the altar of his devotion. His body, still warm, was a new source of materials, a fresh palette for his art. He worked through the night, the rhythmic sounds of his work a grotesque symphony in the aural void of the basement. He harvested what he needed, his movements precise and clinical, his mind a calm, placid sea.

He was so close now. The vessel was almost complete. It was a masterpiece of devotion, a testament to a love that transcended death, that laughed in the face of nature's laws. He had built her a new body, a stronger body, a body that would never fail her again. All that was left was to rejuvenate her mind, to prepare her brain for its triumphant return.

The whispers from the cooler had grown stronger, more insistent. *It's almost time, my darling. You've been so good, so patient. Just one more thing, my sweet, faithful lamb. One more sacrifice to make me whole again.*

He knew what he had to do. He had known it all along, in the deepest, darkest recesses of his fractured mind. The final piece of the puzzle, the ultimate expression of his love, was waiting for him upstairs, locked in her room. His sister. The final lamb to be brought to the slaughter. He ascended the basement stairs, his steps light, his heart filled with a terrible, ecstatic joy. Soon, they would all be reunited. Soon, his mother would be home. The thought was a comforting balm to his ravaged soul, a beacon of light in the all-consuming darkness of his madness.

(CONTENT END)

File: storage/internal/pages/custom/writing/books/hs/omom/chapter_3.md
