    <script type="module">
        import { codeToHtml } from 'https://esm.sh/shiki@1.0.0';

        const SUPABASE_URL = "https://wtasesmqwpnbwzdynnas.supabase.co";
        const SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = "sb_publishable_ay0PuIePjZwrEgP5XpD5iQ_W5wC-5g9";

        const supabaseClient = supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_ANON_KEY);

        let blogsData = [];
        let isAdmin = false;
        let activeEditId = null;
        let isShikiWrapEnabled = localStorage.getItem('shikiWrapEnabled') !== 'false';
        let currentRenderId = 0;

        marked.use({
            breaks: true, gfm: true, async: true,
            async walkTokens(token) {
                if (token.type === 'code') {
                    const shikiHtml = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: token.lang || 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    const header = `<div class="shiki-header"><span class="shiki-lang">${token.lang || 'text'}</span><div class="shiki-actions"><button class="shiki-btn wrap-btn">Wrap</button><button class="shiki-btn copy-btn">Copy</button></div></div>`;
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = `<div class="shiki-container">${header}${shikiHtml}</div>`;
                } else if (token.type === 'codespan') {
                    const raw = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    const inline = raw.replace(/<pre[^>]*>/, '').replace('</pre>', '').replace('<code', '<code class="shiki-inline"');
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = inline;
                }
            }
        });

        async function initAuth() {
            const { data: { session } } = await supabaseClient.auth.getSession();
            handleUserSession(session);
            supabaseClient.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
                handleUserSession(session);
            });
        }

        function handleUserSession(session) {
            if (session && session.user && session.user.email.toLowerCase() === '3rr0r.d3v@gmail.com') {
                isAdmin = true;
                document.body.classList.add('is-admin');
            } else {
                isAdmin = false;
                document.body.classList.remove('is-admin');
            }
            renderBlogs(blogsData);
        }

        function parseDate(dateStr) {
            const [day, month, year] = dateStr.split('/').map(Number);
            return new Date(year, month - 1, day);
        }

        async function renderBlogs(blogs) {
            const renderId = ++currentRenderId;
            const container = document.getElementById('blog-posts');
            container.innerHTML = '';
            for (const blog of blogs) {
                if (renderId !== currentRenderId) return;
                const blogPost = document.createElement('div');
                blogPost.className = 'blog-post';
                blogPost.id = `blog-${blog.id}`;
                const htmlContent = await marked.parse(blog.content);
                if (renderId !== currentRenderId) return;
                blogPost.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="blog-id">#${blog.id}</div>
                    <div class="blog-header">
                        <a href="#" class="blog-title" id="title-anchor-${blog.id}">${blog.title}</a>
                        <div class="blog-date">${blog.date}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="blog-content">${htmlContent}</div>
                    <div class="admin-action-row">
                        <button class="admin-btn" id="edit-btn-${blog.id}">Edit</button>
                        <button class="admin-btn danger-btn" id="del-btn-${blog.id}">Delete</button>
                    </div>
                `;
                container.appendChild(blogPost);

                const titleAnchor = document.getElementById(`title-anchor-${blog.id}`);
                if (titleAnchor) {
                    titleAnchor.onclick = (e) => window.copyBlogLink(e, blog.id);
                }

                const editBtn = document.getElementById(`edit-btn-${blog.id}`);
                if (editBtn) {
                    editBtn.onclick = () => openEditBlogModal(blog);
                }

                const delBtn = document.getElementById(`del-btn-${blog.id}`);
                if (delBtn) {
                    delBtn.onclick = () => deleteBlogPost(blog.id);
                }
            }
            setupShikiInteractions();
        }

        function setupShikiInteractions() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.shiki-container').forEach(container => {
                const wrapBtn = container.querySelector('.wrap-btn');
                if (isShikiWrapEnabled) {
                    container.classList.add('wrap-enabled');
                    if (wrapBtn) { wrapBtn.classList.add('active'); wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: On'; }
                } else {
                    if (wrapBtn) wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: Off';
                }
            });
        }

        function scrollToBlogId(id) {
            const el = document.getElementById(`blog-${id}`);
            if (el) {
                el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                el.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--accent))';
                setTimeout(() => el.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--border))', 2000);
            } else {
                alert(`Blog #${id} not found.`);
            }
        }

        async function syncToSupabase() {
            const { error } = await supabaseClient
                .from('site_content')
                .update({ data: blogsData })
                .eq('key', 'blogs');
            if (error) {
                alert("Error saving: " + error.message);
            }
        }

        window.openAddBlogModal = () => {
            activeEditId = null;
            document.getElementById('modal-title-label').textContent = "Create Blog Post";
            document.getElementById('blog-title-input').value = "";
            document.getElementById('blog-content-input').value = "";
            document.getElementById('blog-modal').classList.add('active');
        };

        function openEditBlogModal(blog) {
            activeEditId = blog.id;
            document.getElementById('modal-title-label').textContent = `Edit Blog Post #${blog.id}`;
            document.getElementById('blog-title-input').value = blog.title;
            document.getElementById('blog-content-input').value = blog.content;
            document.getElementById('blog-modal').classList.add('active');
        }

        window.closeBlogModal = () => {
            document.getElementById('blog-modal').classList.remove('active');
        };

        async function handleSaveBlog() {
            const title = document.getElementById('blog-title-input').value.trim();
            const content = document.getElementById('blog-content-input').value.trim();
            if (!title || !content) return;

            if (activeEditId !== null) {
                const blog = blogsData.find(b => b.id === activeEditId);
                if (blog) {
                    blog.title = title;
                    blog.content = content;
                }
            } else {
                const nextId = blogsData.length > 0 ? Math.max(...blogsData.map(b => b.id)) + 1 : 1;
                const today = new Date();
                const dateStr = `${String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}/${String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}/${today.getFullYear()}`;
                
                blogsData.unshift({
                    id: nextId,
                    date: dateStr,
                    title,
                    content
                });
            }

            closeBlogModal();
            await syncToSupabase();
        }

        async function deleteBlogPost(id) {
            if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to delete Blog Post #${id}?`)) return;
            blogsData = blogsData.filter(b => b.id !== id);
            await syncToSupabase();
        }

        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.matches('.shiki-btn.copy-btn')) {
                const container = e.target.closest('.shiki-container');
                const codeBlock = container?.querySelector('pre.shiki code');
                if (codeBlock) {
                    navigator.clipboard.writeText(codeBlock.innerText).then(() => {
                        e.target.textContent = 'Copied!';
                        setTimeout(() => e.target.textContent = 'Copy', 2000);
                    });
                }
            }
            if (e.target.matches('.shiki-btn.wrap-btn')) {
                isShikiWrapEnabled = !isShikiWrapEnabled;
                localStorage.setItem('shikiWrapEnabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                document.querySelectorAll('.shiki-container').forEach(container => {
                    const wrapBtn = container.querySelector('.wrap-btn');
                    container.classList.toggle('wrap-enabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                    if (wrapBtn) {
                        wrapBtn.classList.toggle('active', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                        wrapBtn.textContent = isShikiWrapEnabled ? 'Wrap: On' : 'Wrap: Off';
                    }
                });
            }

            const link = e.target.closest('a');
            if (link) {
                const href = link.getAttribute('href');
                if (!href) return;

                if (href.match(/^~\/&id=(\d+)$/)) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const id = href.split('=')[1];
                    scrollToBlogId(id);
                    return;
                }

                if (href.startsWith('./#')) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const hash = href.substring(2); 
                    window.parent.location.hash = hash;
                    return;
                }
            }
        });

        window.copyBlogLink = (e, id) => { e.preventDefault(); const url = `https://devicals.github.io/#page=blogs&id=${id}`; navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(() => { e.target.textContent = "Link Copied!"; setTimeout(() => { e.target.textContent = blogsData.find(b=>b.id===id).title; }, 2000); }); document.getElementById(`blog-${id}`).scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); };
        window.jumpToBlog = () => { 
            const id = document.getElementById('blog-id-input').value; 
            if (!id) return; 
            scrollToBlogId(id);
        };
        window.copyRSS = () => { const url = "https://github.com/devicals/devicals.github.io/raw/refs/heads/main/storage/internal/blogs.xml"; navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(() => { const btn = document.getElementById('rss-btn'); btn.textContent = 'Copied!'; setTimeout(() => { btn.textContent = 'RSS URL'; }, 2000); }); };

        document.getElementById('blog-save-submit').onclick = handleSaveBlog;

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
            try {
                const { data, error } = await supabaseClient
                    .from('site_content')
                    .select('data')
                    .eq('key', 'blogs')
                    .single();

                if (data && data.data) {
                    blogsData = data.data.sort((a, b) => parseDate(b.date) - parseDate(a.date));
                    await renderBlogs(blogsData);
                }

                supabaseClient
                    .channel('blogs-realtime')
                    .on(
                        'postgres_changes',
                        { event: 'UPDATE', schema: 'public', table: 'site_content', filter: 'key=eq.blogs' },
                        async (payload) => {
                            if (payload.new && payload.new.data) {
                                blogsData = payload.new.data.sort((a, b) => parseDate(b.date) - parseDate(a.date));
                                await renderBlogs(blogsData);
                            }
                        }
                    )
                    .subscribe();

                await initAuth();

                const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.hash.substring(1));
                const id = params.get('id');
                if (id) setTimeout(() => { const el = document.getElementById(`blog-${id}`); if (el) el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); }, 500);
            } catch (error) { console.error(error); }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

(CONTENT END)

    <script>
        const SUPABASE_URL = "https://wtasesmqwpnbwzdynnas.supabase.co";
        const SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = "sb_publishable_ay0PuIePjZwrEgP5XpD5iQ_W5wC-5g9";

        const supabaseClient = supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_ANON_KEY);

        let messagesList = [];
        let isAdmin = false;
        let isEraserActive = false;
        let previousColor = '#000000';
        
        const canvas = document.getElementById('drawing-canvas');
        const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        let isDrawing = false;
        let isCanvasDirty = false;

        let undoStack = [];
        let redoStack = [];

        function saveCanvasState() {
            if (undoStack.length > 20) undoStack.shift();
            undoStack.push(ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height));
            redoStack = [];
        }

        function undo() {
            if (undoStack.length > 1) {
                redoStack.push(undoStack.pop());
                const state = undoStack[undoStack.length - 1];
                ctx.putImageData(state, 0, 0);
            }
        }

        function redo() {
            if (redoStack.length > 0) {
                const state = redoStack.pop();
                undoStack.push(state);
                ctx.putImageData(state, 0, 0);
            }
        }

        window.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
            if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'z') {
                e.preventDefault();
                undo();
            }
            if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'y') {
                e.preventDefault();
                redo();
            }
        });

        function resizeCanvas() {
            const rect = canvas.parentNode.getBoundingClientRect();
            canvas.width = rect.width;
            canvas.height = rect.height;
            ctx.lineCap = 'round';
            ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
            clearCanvas();
            saveCanvasState();
        }

        function clearCanvas() {
            ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
            ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
            isCanvasDirty = false;
        }

        function fillCanvas() {
            saveCanvasState();
            ctx.fillStyle = document.getElementById('brush-color').value;
            ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
            isCanvasDirty = true;
        }

        function toggleEraser() {
            isEraserActive = !isEraserActive;
            const btn = document.getElementById('eraser-btn');
            const colorInput = document.getElementById('brush-color');
            if (isEraserActive) {
                previousColor = colorInput.value;
                colorInput.value = '#ffffff';
                btn.classList.add('active');
            } else {
                colorInput.value = previousColor;
                btn.classList.remove('active');
            }
        }

        function toggleCanvas() {
            const sec = document.getElementById('canvas-section');
            const btn = document.getElementById('toggle-canvas-btn');
            sec.classList.toggle('active');
            if (sec.classList.contains('active')) {
                btn.textContent = "- Remove Drawing";
                setTimeout(resizeCanvas, 50);
            } else {
                btn.textContent = "+ Add Drawing";
                clearCanvas();
                undoStack = [];
                redoStack = [];
            }
        }

        function getMousePos(e) {
            const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
            const clientX = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
            const clientY = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;
            return {
                x: (clientX - rect.left) * (canvas.width / rect.width),
                y: (clientY - rect.top) * (canvas.height / rect.height)
            };
        }

        function startDraw(e) {
            saveCanvasState();
            isDrawing = true;
            isCanvasDirty = true;
            const pos = getMousePos(e);
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.moveTo(pos.x, pos.y);
            draw(e);
        }

        function draw(e) {
            if (!isDrawing) return;
            e.preventDefault();
            const pos = getMousePos(e);
            ctx.lineTo(pos.x, pos.y);
            ctx.strokeStyle = document.getElementById('brush-color').value;
            ctx.lineWidth = document.getElementById('brush-size').value;
            ctx.stroke();
        }

        function stopDrawing() {
            isDrawing = false;
        }

        canvas.addEventListener('mousedown', startDraw);
        canvas.addEventListener('mousemove', draw);
        window.addEventListener('mouseup', stopDrawing);

        canvas.addEventListener('touchstart', startDraw, { passive: false });
        canvas.addEventListener('touchmove', draw, { passive: false });
        window.addEventListener('touchend', stopDrawing, { passive: true });

        window.clearCanvas = clearCanvas;

        async function initAuth() {
            const { data: { session } } = await supabaseClient.auth.getSession();
            handleUserSession(session);
            supabaseClient.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
                handleUserSession(session);
            });
        }

        function handleUserSession(session) {
            if (session && session.user && session.user.email.toLowerCase() === '3rr0r.d3v@gmail.com') {
                isAdmin = true;
                document.body.classList.add('is-admin');
                document.getElementById('creator-badge-cb').checked = true;
            } else {
                isAdmin = false;
                document.body.classList.remove('is-admin');
            }
            if (messagesList) renderMessages();
        }

        async function initDatabase() {
            const { data } = await supabaseClient
                .from('guestbook')
                .select('*')
                .order('created_at', { ascending: false });

            if (data) {
                messagesList = data;
                renderMessages();
            }

            supabaseClient
                .channel('guestbook-realtime')
                .on(
                    'postgres_changes',
                    { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'guestbook' },
                    async () => {
                        const { data } = await supabaseClient.from('guestbook').select('*');
                        if (data) {
                            messagesList = data;
                            renderMessages();
                        }
                    }
                )
                .subscribe();
        }

        function renderMessages() {
            const container = document.getElementById('chat-messages');
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            messagesList.sort((a,b) => new Date(a.created_at) - new Date(b.created_at)).forEach((msg) => {
                const bubble = document.createElement('div');
                const isOwn = msg.name === 'Error Dev' || msg.is_creator;
                bubble.className = 'chat-bubble' + (isOwn ? ' is-own' : '');
                
                const date = new Date(msg.created_at).toLocaleDateString(undefined, {
                    month: 'short', day: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'
                });

                bubble.innerHTML = `
                    ${isAdmin ? `
                    <div class="chat-bubble-actions">
                        <button class="chat-bubble-del" onclick="deleteMessage(${msg.id})">✕</button>
                    </div>` : ''}
                    <div class="chat-meta">
                        <span class="poster-name-wrapper">
                            <strong>${escapeHTML(msg.name)}</strong>
                            <span class="ip-tooltip">IP: ${msg.ip_address || 'Hidden'}</span>
                        </span>
                        ${msg.is_creator ? `<span class="creator-badge">Creator</span>` : ''}
                        ${msg.country && msg.country !== 'Unknown' ? `<span class="country-badge">${escapeHTML(msg.country)}</span>` : ''}
                        • ${date}
                    </div>
                    ${msg.message ? `<div class="chat-text">${escapeHTML(msg.message)}</div>` : ''}
                    ${msg.drawing ? `<img class="chat-drawing" src="${msg.drawing}">` : ''}
                `;
                container.appendChild(bubble);
            });
            container.scrollTop = container.scrollHeight;
        }

        function escapeHTML(str) {
            return str.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
        }

        window.sendChitChat = async () => {
            const nameInput = document.getElementById('chat-name');
            const msgInput = document.getElementById('chat-msg');
            const creatorCb = document.getElementById('creator-badge-cb');
            
            const name = nameInput.value.trim() || 'Anonymous';
            const message = msgInput.value.trim();
            
            let drawing = null;
            if (isCanvasDirty) {
                drawing = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
            }

            if (!message && !drawing) return;

            localStorage.setItem('chitchat_user_name', nameInput.value.trim());

            let ip = 'Hidden';
            let country = 'Unknown';
            let isVpn = false;
            
            try {
                const ipResp = await fetch('https://ipapi.co/json/');
                const ipData = await ipResp.json();
                if (ipData) {
                    ip = ipData.ip || 'Hidden';
                    country = ipData.country_name || 'Unknown';
                    const org = (ipData.org || '').toLowerCase();
                    isVpn = org.includes('vpn') || org.includes('hosting') || org.includes('server') || org.includes('tor') || org.includes('cloud') || org.includes('proxy');
                }
            } catch(e) {}

            const isCreatorChecked = isAdmin && creatorCb && creatorCb.checked;

            const { data, error } = await supabaseClient
                .from('guestbook')
                .insert({ 
                    name, 
                    message: message || null, 
                    drawing,
                    is_creator: isCreatorChecked,
                    ip_address: ip,
                    country,
                    is_vpn: isVpn
                })
                .select('id')
                .single();

            if (error) {
                alert("Error sending message: " + error.message);
            } else {
                msgInput.value = '';
                if (document.getElementById('canvas-section').classList.contains('active')) {
                    toggleCanvas();
                } else {
                    clearCanvas();
                }
            }
        };

        window.deleteMessage = async (id) => {
            if (!isAdmin) return;
            if (!confirm("Are you sure you want to delete this message?")) return;
            
            const { error } = await supabaseClient
                .from('guestbook')
                .delete()
                .eq('id', id);

            if (error) {
                alert("Error deleting: " + error.message);
            }
        };

        window.addEventListener('resize', resizeCanvas);

        window.addEventListener('message', (e) => {
            if (e.data && e.data.type === 'auth-sync') {
                handleUserSession(e.data.session);
            }
        });

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            const savedName = localStorage.getItem('chitchat_user_name');
            if (savedName) {
                document.getElementById('chat-name').value = savedName;
            }
            initDatabase();
            initAuth();
            setTimeout(resizeCanvas, 100);
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

(CONTENT END)

    <style>

<body>
    <div class="page-container">
        <h1 class="page-title" id="page-title">Loading...</h1>
        <div id="breadcrumb" class="breadcrumb">
            <div class="breadcrumb-path" id="breadcrumb-path"></div>
            <div class="breadcrumb-nav">
                <button class="breadcrumb-btn" id="prev-btn" disabled>← Prev</button>
                <button class="breadcrumb-btn" id="next-btn" disabled>Next →</button>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div id="content"></div>
        <button class="scroll-to-top" id="scroll-to-top">↑ Top</button>

    <script type="module">
        import { codeToHtml } from 'https://esm.sh/shiki@1.0.0';
        let currentPath = [];
        let customPageData = null;
        let rootPageId = null;
        let isShikiWrapEnabled = localStorage.getItem('shikiWrapEnabled') !== 'false';
        marked.use({
            breaks: true, gfm: true, async: true,
            async walkTokens(token) {
                if (token.type === 'code') {
                    const shikiHtml = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: token.lang || 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = `<div class="shiki-container"><div class="shiki-header"><span class="shiki-lang">${token.lang || 'text'}</span><div class="shiki-actions"><button class="shiki-btn wrap-btn">Wrap</button><button class="shiki-btn copy-btn">Copy</button></div></div>${shikiHtml}</div>`;
                } else if (token.type === 'codespan') {
                    const raw = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    const inline = raw.replace(/<pre[^>]*>/, '').replace('</pre>', '').replace('<code', '<code class="shiki-inline"');
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = inline;
                }
            }
        });
        function normalizePath(path) {
            const parts = path.split('/');
            const stack = [];
            for (const part of parts) {
                if (part === '..') { if (stack.length > 0) stack.pop(); } 
                else if (part !== '.' && part !== '') { stack.push(part); }
            }
            return (path.startsWith('/') ? '/' : '') + stack.join('/');
        }
        function resolvePath(relativePath, baseDir) {
            if (relativePath.startsWith('~/')) return normalizePath('/storage/internal/pages/custom/' + relativePath.substring(2));
            if (relativePath.startsWith('/')) return normalizePath(relativePath);
            return normalizePath(baseDir + relativePath);
        }
        async function loadYAML(path) {
            try {
                const resp = await fetch(path);
                if (!resp.ok) return null;
                return jsyaml.load(await resp.text());
            } catch (e) { return null; }
        }
        function getParentParams() { return new URLSearchParams(window.parent.location.hash.substring(1)); }
        function buildNavURL(path) { return `#page=${rootPageId}${path.length > 0 ? '&nav=' + path.map(p => p.id).join('>') : ''}`; }
        window.navigateTo = async function(path) {
            currentPath = path;
            updateBreadcrumb();
            window.parent.history.replaceState(null, null, buildNavURL(path));
            const content = document.getElementById('content');
            const breadcrumb = document.getElementById('breadcrumb');
            let isInterests = false;
            if (path.length === 0) {
                const typeInfo = typeof customPageData.type === 'object' ? customPageData.type.type : customPageData.type;
                if (typeInfo === 'interests') {
                    isInterests = true;
                    content.innerHTML = `<iframe id="viewer-frame" src="/storage/internal/pages/main/interests.html?file=${encodeURIComponent(customPageData.path)}"></iframe>`;
                } else {
                    await renderSections(customPageData.path);
                }
            } else {
                const item = path[path.length - 1];
                const fullPageId = `${rootPageId}_${path.map(p => p.id).join('_')}`;
                if (item.locked && sessionStorage.getItem('unlocked_' + fullPageId) !== 'true') {
                    content.innerHTML = `<div class="card" style="text-align: center;"><h2>Page Locked</h2><p>This content is locked.</p><button class="breadcrumb-btn" onclick="requestParentUnlock('${fullPageId}')">Unlock</button></div>`;
                    return;
                }
                if (item.type === 'section') {
                    await renderSections(item.path);
                } else if (item.type === 'interests') {
                    isInterests = true;
                    content.innerHTML = `<iframe id="viewer-frame" src="/storage/internal/pages/main/interests.html?file=${encodeURIComponent(item.path)}"></iframe>`;
                } else if (item.type === 'md') {
                    const resp = await fetch(item.path);
                    if (resp.ok) {
                        let html = await marked.parse(await resp.text());
                        html = html.replace(/<a href="::([^"]+)">([^<]+)<\/a>/g, '<span class="md-swap"><span class="original-text">$2</span><span class="swap-text">$1</span></span>');
                        content.innerHTML = `<div class="md-content">${html}</div>`;
                        setupShikiInteractions();
                    }
                } else if (item.type === 'raw') {
                    window.parent.location.href = `/storage/internal/pages/main/raw.html?file=${encodeURIComponent(item.path)}`;
                }
            }
            breadcrumb.style.display = isInterests ? 'none' : 'flex';
            await updateNavButtons();
        };
        function updateBreadcrumb() {
            const container = document.getElementById('breadcrumb-path');
            if (!customPageData) return;
            container.innerHTML = '';
            const rootLink = document.createElement('a');
            rootLink.textContent = customPageData.name;
            rootLink.onclick = () => navigateTo([]);
            container.appendChild(rootLink);
            currentPath.forEach((item, i) => {
                const pathSlice = currentPath.slice(0, i + 1);
                container.appendChild(Object.assign(document.createElement('span'), {textContent: ' / '}));
                const link = document.createElement('a');
                link.textContent = item.name;
                link.onclick = () => navigateTo(pathSlice);
                container.appendChild(link);
            });
        }
        async function updateNavButtons() {
            const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prev-btn'), nextBtn = document.getElementById('next-btn');
            prevBtn.disabled = nextBtn.disabled = true;
            if (currentPath.length === 0) return;
            const parentYaml = currentPath.length === 1 ? customPageData.path : currentPath[currentPath.length - 2].path;
            const parentData = await loadYAML(parentYaml);
            if (!parentData?.pages) return;
            const isRevealed = sessionStorage.getItem('sidebar_expire') && Date.now() < parseInt(sessionStorage.getItem('sidebar_expire'));
            const siblings = parentData.pages.filter(p => isRevealed || !p.hidden);
            const idx = siblings.findIndex(p => String(p.id) === String(currentPath[currentPath.length - 1].id));
            const navSib = (sib) => {
                const base = parentYaml.substring(0, parentYaml.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
                const type = (typeof sib.type === 'object' ? sib.type.type : sib.type) || (sib.path.endsWith('.yaml') ? 'section' : 'md');
                navigateTo([...currentPath.slice(0, -1), { id: String(sib.id), name: sib.name, path: resolvePath(sib.path, base), type, hidden: sib.hidden||false, locked: sib.locked||false }]);
            };
            if (idx > 0) { prevBtn.disabled = false; prevBtn.onclick = () => navSib(siblings[idx-1]); }
            if (idx < siblings.length - 1) { nextBtn.disabled = false; nextBtn.onclick = () => navSib(siblings[idx+1]); }
        }
        async function parseURLNav() {
            const params = getParentParams();
            const nav = (params.get('nav') || "").split('>').filter(x => x);
            const path = [];
            let curYaml = customPageData.path;
            for (const id of nav) {
                const data = await loadYAML(curYaml);
                const p = data?.pages?.find(x => String(x.id) === id);
                if (!p) break;
                const base = curYaml.substring(0, curYaml.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
                const resolved = resolvePath(p.path, base);
                const type = (typeof p.type === 'object' ? p.type.type : p.type) || (p.path.endsWith('.yaml') ? 'section' : 'md');
                path.push({ id: String(p.id), name: p.name, path: resolved, type, hidden: p.hidden||false, locked: p.locked||false });
                if (type === 'section') curYaml = resolved;
            }
            return path;
        }
        async function renderSections(yamlPath) {
            const data = await loadYAML(yamlPath);
            if (!data) return;
            const baseDir = yamlPath.substring(0, yamlPath.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
            const grid = document.createElement('div');
            grid.className = 'section-grid';
            const isRevealed = sessionStorage.getItem('sidebar_expire') && Date.now() < parseInt(sessionStorage.getItem('sidebar_expire'));
            data.pages.filter(p => isRevealed || !p.hidden).forEach(p => {
                const card = document.createElement('a');
                card.className = 'section-card';
                card.onclick = () => {
                    const type = (typeof p.type === 'object' ? p.type.type : p.type) || (p.path.endsWith('.yaml') ? 'section' : 'md');
                    navigateTo([...currentPath, { id: String(p.id), name: p.name, path: resolvePath(p.path, baseDir), type, hidden: p.hidden||false, locked: p.locked||false }]);
                };
                const tObj = typeof p.type === 'object' ? p.type : { type: p.type || 'SECTION' };
                const tName = (tObj.type || 'SECTION').toUpperCase();
                card.innerHTML = `<div class="section-card-title">${p.name}</div><div class="section-card-type">${tObj.display ? `(${tName}) ${tObj.display.toUpperCase()}` : tName}</div>`;
                grid.appendChild(card);
            });
            document.getElementById('content').replaceChildren(grid);
        }
        function setupShikiInteractions() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.shiki-container').forEach(c => {
                const btn = c.querySelector('.wrap-btn');
                c.classList.toggle('wrap-enabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                if (btn) { btn.classList.toggle('active', isShikiWrapEnabled); btn.textContent = isShikiWrapEnabled ? 'Wrap: On' : 'Wrap: Off'; }
            });
        }
        async function init() {
            rootPageId = getParentParams().get('page');
            const custom = await loadYAML('/storage/data/custom.yaml');
            for (const k in custom.customPages) {
                const sub = custom.customPages[k].sub;
                const found = sub?.find(p => p.id === rootPageId);
                if (found) { customPageData = { ...found, path: resolvePath(found.path, '/storage/internal/pages/custom/') }; break; }
            }
            if (!customPageData) return;
            document.getElementById('page-title').textContent = customPageData.name;
            navigateTo(await parseURLNav());
        }
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.matches('.copy-btn')) {
                const code = e.target.closest('.shiki-container').querySelector('code').innerText;
                navigator.clipboard.writeText(code).then(() => { e.target.textContent = 'Copied!'; setTimeout(() => e.target.textContent = 'Copy', 2000); });
            }
            if (e.target.matches('.wrap-btn')) {
                isShikiWrapEnabled = !isShikiWrapEnabled;
                localStorage.setItem('shikiWrapEnabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                setupShikiInteractions();
            }
        });
        window.addEventListener('scroll', () => document.getElementById('scroll-to-top').classList.toggle('visible', window.scrollY > 300));
        document.getElementById('scroll-to-top').onclick = () => window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
        window.addEventListener('hashchange', async () => {
            const n = await parseURLNav();
            if (JSON.stringify(n) !== JSON.stringify(currentPath)) navigateTo(n);
        });
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

(CONTENT END)

    <div id="copy-toast">LINK COPIED TO CLIPBOARD</div>
    
    <div class="page-container">

    <!-- Download Editor Modal -->
    <div id="download-modal" class="modal">
        <div class="modal-content">
            <div class="modal-header">
                <h2 id="modal-title-label">Create Download Card</h2>
                <button class="modal-close" onclick="closeDownloadModal()">×</button>
            </div>
            <div class="modal-body">
                <input type="text" id="dl-name-input" placeholder="Title/Name">
                <textarea id="dl-desc-input" placeholder="Description"></textarea>
                <input type="text" id="dl-url-input" placeholder="Download URL">
                <button class="btn-primary" onclick="handleSaveDownload()" style="width: 100%; padding: 10px;">Save Download</button>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    
    <script>
        const SUPABASE_URL = "https://wtasesmqwpnbwzdynnas.supabase.co";
        const SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = "sb_publishable_ay0PuIePjZwrEgP5XpD5iQ_W5wC-5g9";

        const supabaseClient = supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_ANON_KEY);

        let downloadsData = [];
        let isAdmin = false;
        let activeEditId = null;

        async function initAuth() {
            const { data: { session } } = await supabaseClient.auth.getSession();
            handleUserSession(session);
            supabaseClient.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
                handleUserSession(session);
            });
        }

        function handleUserSession(session) {
            if (session && session.user && session.user.email.toLowerCase() === '3rr0r.d3v@gmail.com') {
                isAdmin = true;
                document.body.classList.add('is-admin');
            } else {
                isAdmin = false;
                document.body.classList.remove('is-admin');
            }
            renderDownloads();
        }

        async function initDatabase() {
            const { data, error } = await supabaseClient
                .from('site_content')
                .select('data')
                .eq('key', 'downloads')
                .single();

            if (data && data.data) {
                downloadsData = data.data;
                renderDownloads();
            }

            supabaseClient
                .channel('downloads-realtime')
                .on(
                    'postgres_changes',
                    { event: 'UPDATE', schema: 'public', table: 'site_content', filter: 'key=eq.downloads' },
                    (payload) => {
                        if (payload.new && payload.new.data) {
                            downloadsData = payload.new.data;
                            renderDownloads();
                        }
                    }
                )
                .subscribe();
        }

        async function syncToSupabase() {
            if (!isAdmin) return;
            const { error } = await supabaseClient
                .from('site_content')
                .update({ data: downloadsData })
                .eq('key', 'downloads');
            if (error) {
                alert("Error saving: " + error.message);
            }
        }

        function renderDownloads() {
            const container = document.getElementById('downloads-list');
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            downloadsData.forEach((download, idx) => {
                const card = document.createElement('div');
                card.className = 'download-card';
                card.id = `download-${download.id}`;
                
                card.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="download-header">
                        <div class="download-left" onclick="copyLink(${download.id})" title="Click to copy link">
                            <span class="download-id">#${download.id}</span>
                            <span class="download-name">${download.name}</span>
                        </div>
                        <a href="${download.url}" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="download-btn">Download</a>
                    </div>
                    <div class="download-description">${download.description}</div>
                    <div class="admin-action-row">
                        <button class="admin-btn" onclick="openEditDownloadModal(${idx})">Edit</button>
                        <button class="admin-btn danger-btn" onclick="deleteDownload(${download.id})">Delete</button>
                    </div>
                `;
                container.appendChild(card);
            });
            handleHash();
        }

        function copyLink(id) {
            const baseUrl = window.parent.location.origin + window.parent.location.pathname;
            const newHash = `page=downloads&id=${id}`;
            const fullUrl = `${baseUrl}#${newHash}`;
            
            window.parent.history.replaceState(null, null, `#${newHash}`);
            
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(fullUrl).then(() => {
                const toast = document.getElementById('copy-toast');
                toast.textContent = `LINK COPIED [#${id}]`;
                toast.style.display = 'block';
                setTimeout(() => { toast.style.display = 'none'; }, 2000);
            });

            document.querySelectorAll('.download-card').forEach(card => card.style.borderColor = '');
            
            const activeCard = document.getElementById(`download-${id}`);
            if (activeCard) {
                activeCard.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--accent))';
                setTimeout(() => { activeCard.style.borderColor = ''; }, 1000);
            }
        }

        function handleHash() {
            const hash = window.location.hash.substring(1);
            const params = new URLSearchParams(hash);
            const id = params.get('id');
            if (id) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    const element = document.getElementById(`download-${id}`);
                    if (element) {
                        element.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                        element.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--accent))';
                        setTimeout(() => { element.style.borderColor = ''; }, 1000);
                    }
                }, 300);
            }
        }

        window.openAddDownloadModal = () => {
            activeEditId = null;
            document.getElementById('modal-title-label').textContent = "Create Download Card";
            document.getElementById('dl-name-input').value = "";
            document.getElementById('dl-desc-input').value = "";
            document.getElementById('dl-url-input').value = "";
            document.getElementById('download-modal').classList.add('active');
        };

        window.openEditDownloadModal = (idx) => {
            const dl = downloadsData[idx];
            activeEditId = dl.id;
            document.getElementById('modal-title-label').textContent = `Edit Download Card #${dl.id}`;
            document.getElementById('dl-name-input').value = dl.name;
            document.getElementById('dl-desc-input').value = dl.description;
            document.getElementById('dl-url-input').value = dl.url;
            document.getElementById('download-modal').classList.add('active');
        };

        window.closeDownloadModal = () => {
            document.getElementById('download-modal').classList.remove('active');
        };

        window.handleSaveDownload = async () => {
            const name = document.getElementById('dl-name-input').value.trim();
            const description = document.getElementById('dl-desc-input').value.trim();
            const url = document.getElementById('dl-url-input').value.trim();
            if (!name || !url) return;

            if (activeEditId !== null) {
                const dl = downloadsData.find(d => d.id === activeEditId);
                if (dl) {
                    dl.name = name;
                    dl.description = description;
                    dl.url = url;
                }
            } else {
                const nextId = downloadsData.length > 0 ? Math.max(...downloadsData.map(d => d.id)) + 1 : 1;
                downloadsData.push({ id: nextId, name, description, url });
            }

            closeDownloadModal();
            await syncToSupabase();
        };

        window.deleteDownload = async (id) => {
            if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to delete download card #${id}?`)) return;
            downloadsData = downloadsData.filter(d => d.id !== id);
            await syncToSupabase();
        };

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            initDatabase();
            initAuth();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

(CONTENT END)

<body>
    <div id="copy-toast">LINK COPIED TO CLIPBOARD</div>
    <div class="page-container">
        <h1 class="page-title" id="gallery-title">Gallery</h1>
        
        <div class="filter-box" id="filter-box">
            <div class="filter-toggle" id="filter-toggle" onclick="toggleFilter()">&lt;</div>
            <span class="filter-label">GALLERY FILTER</span>
            
            <label id="label-img" style="display:none">
                <input type="checkbox" id="filter-img" checked onchange="applyFilters()"> IMAGES
            </label>
            <label id="label-video" style="display:none">
                <input type="checkbox" id="filter-video" checked onchange="applyFilters()"> VIDEOS
            </label>
            <label id="label-audio" style="display:none">
                <input type="checkbox" id="filter-audio" checked onchange="applyFilters()"> AUDIO
            </label>

            <div class="jump-container">
                <span class="filter-label">JUMP TO ID</span>
                <input type="number" id="jump-id-input" class="jump-input" placeholder="ID #">
                <button class="jump-btn" onclick="executeJump()">Jump</button>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="gallery-grid" id="gallery-grid"></div>
    </div>
    
    <script>
        let galleryData = [];
        let imgExtensions = [];
        let videoExtensions = [];
        let audioExtensions = [];
        let galleryType = 'gallery';
        let currentPageId = '';
        let yamlFilePath = '';

        async function parseExtensionList(path) {
            try {
                const resp = await fetch(path);
                if (!resp.ok) return [];
                const text = await resp.text();
                const regex = /\(([\s\S]*?)\)/;
                const match = text.match(regex);
                if (!match) return [];
                return match[1].split(/[,\n]/).map(s => s.trim().replace(/["']/g, '')).filter(s => s.length > 0);
            } catch (e) { return []; }
        }

        function getItemType(filename) {
            if (!filename) return 'NONE';
            const ext = filename.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            if (imgExtensions.includes(ext)) return 'IMAGE';
            if (videoExtensions.includes(ext)) return 'VIDEO';
            if (audioExtensions.includes(ext)) return 'AUDIO';
            return 'UNKNOWN';
        }

        async function loadGallery() {
            const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            yamlFilePath = params.get('file');
            galleryType = params.get('type') || 'gallery';
            const parentHash = window.parent.location.hash.substring(1);
            const parentParams = new URLSearchParams(parentHash);
            currentPageId = parentParams.get('page') || 'home';

            if (!yamlFilePath) return;

            [imgExtensions, videoExtensions, audioExtensions] = await Promise.all([
                parseExtensionList('/storage/internal/ext/image.list'),
                parseExtensionList('/storage/internal/ext/video.list'),
                parseExtensionList('/storage/internal/ext/music.list')
            ]);

            const response = await fetch(yamlFilePath);
            const text = await response.text();
            const data = jsyaml.load(text);
            galleryData = data.items || [];

            renderGallery();
            const jumpId = parentParams.get('id');
            if (jumpId) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    const el = document.getElementById(`item-${jumpId}`);
                    if (el) el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                }, 800);
            }
        }

        function copyLink(id) {
            const newHash = `page=${currentPageId}&id=${id}`;
            const baseUrl = window.parent.location.origin + window.parent.location.pathname;
            const fullUrl = `${baseUrl}#${newHash}`;
            window.parent.history.replaceState(null, null, `#${newHash}`);
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(fullUrl).then(() => {
                const toast = document.getElementById('copy-toast');
                toast.textContent = `LINK COPIED & URL UPDATED [#${id}]`;
                toast.style.display = 'block';
                setTimeout(() => { toast.style.display = 'none'; }, 2000);
            });
            document.querySelectorAll('.gallery-card').forEach(card => card.style.borderColor = '#2d2e2e');
            const activeCard = document.getElementById(`item-${id}`);
            if (activeCard) activeCard.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--accent))';
        }

        function executeJump() {
            const id = document.getElementById('jump-id-input').value;
            const el = document.getElementById(`item-${id}`);
            if (el) {
                el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                el.style.outline = '2px solid hsl(var(--accent))';
                setTimeout(() => el.style.outline = 'none', 2000);
            }
        }

        function renderGallery() {
            const container = document.getElementById('gallery-grid');
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            const showImgs = document.getElementById('filter-img').checked;
            const showVideos = document.getElementById('filter-video').checked;
            const showAudio = document.getElementById('filter-audio').checked;

            let typesFound = { IMAGE: false, VIDEO: false, AUDIO: false };
            const headerItem = galleryData.find(i => i.id === 0);
            if (headerItem) {
                const headCard = document.createElement('div');
                headCard.className = 'gallery-card body-only';
                headCard.id = `item-0`;
                headCard.innerHTML = headerItem.body ? marked.parse(headerItem.body) : '';
                container.appendChild(headCard);
            }

            const yamlBaseDir = yamlFilePath.substring(0, yamlFilePath.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);

            galleryData.forEach((item, index) => {
                if (item.id === 0) return;

                let resolvedPath = item.path;
                if (!item.path.startsWith('/')) {
                    resolvedPath = yamlBaseDir + item.path;
                }
                
                const id = item.id || index;
                const type = getItemType(item.path);

                if (type !== 'UNKNOWN') typesFound[type] = true;
                if (galleryType === 'gallery.img' && type !== 'IMAGE') return;
                if (galleryType === 'gallery.video' && type !== 'VIDEO') return;
                if (galleryType === 'gallery.audio' && type !== 'AUDIO') return;
                
                if (galleryType === 'gallery') {
                    if (type === 'IMAGE' && !showImgs) return;
                    if (type === 'VIDEO' && !showVideos) return;
                    if (type === 'AUDIO' && !showAudio) return;
                }

                const card = document.createElement('div');
                card.className = 'gallery-card';
                card.id = `item-${id}`;
                
                let mediaHtml = '';
                if (type === 'IMAGE') {
                    mediaHtml = `<img src="${resolvedPath}" loading="lazy">`;
                } else if (type === 'VIDEO') {
                    mediaHtml = `<video src="${resolvedPath}" controls preload="metadata"></video>`;
                } else if (type === 'AUDIO') {
                    mediaHtml = `
                        <div class="audio-ui">
                            <div class="audio-error-msg" id="error-${index}"><strong>Cannot find specified audio file.</strong></div>
                            <audio id="aud-${index}" src="${resolvedPath}" preload="metadata"></audio>
                            <div class="audio-controls-row">
                                <button class="audio-btn" id="play-btn-${index}">▶</button>
                                <input type="range" id="seek-${index}" class="audio-progress" value="0" step="0.1" max="100">
                                <button class="audio-btn audio-btn-small" id="repeat-btn-${index}" title="Repeat Once">1</button>
                                <button class="audio-btn audio-btn-small" id="loop-btn-${index}" title="Loop">∞</button>
                            </div>
                            <div class="audio-time-display" id="time-${index}">00:00 / 00:00</div>
                        </div>`;
                }

                card.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="gallery-header">
                        <div class="header-left" onclick="copyLink('${id}')" title="Click to copy link">
                            <span class="gallery-id-label">#${id}</span>
                            <span class="gallery-type-label">${type}</span>
                        </div>
                        <a href="${resolvedPath}" download class="download-btn">Download</a>
                    </div>
                    <div class="gallery-media-container">
                        ${mediaHtml}
                    </div>
                    ${item.title ? `
                    <div class="gallery-info">
                        <div class="gallery-item-title" onclick="copyLink('${id}')">${item.title}</div>
                        ${item.description ? `<div class="gallery-item-desc">${item.description}</div>` : ''}
                    </div>` : ''}
                `;
                container.appendChild(card);

                if (type === 'AUDIO') setupAudioPlayer(index);
            });
            document.getElementById('label-img').style.display = typesFound.IMAGE ? 'flex' : 'none';
            document.getElementById('label-video').style.display = typesFound.VIDEO ? 'flex' : 'none';
            document.getElementById('label-audio').style.display = typesFound.AUDIO ? 'flex' : 'none';
        }

        function setupAudioPlayer(index) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                const aud = document.getElementById(`aud-${index}`);
                const playBtn = document.getElementById(`play-btn-${index}`);
                const seek = document.getElementById(`seek-${index}`);
                const timeDisplay = document.getElementById(`time-${index}`);
                const repeatBtn = document.getElementById(`repeat-btn-${index}`);
                const loopBtn = document.getElementById(`loop-btn-${index}`);
                const errorDisplay = document.getElementById(`error-${index}`);
                let repeatOnce = false;
                
                const formatTime = (s) => isNaN(s) || s === Infinity ? '00:00' : `${Math.floor(s/60).toString().padStart(2,'0')}:${Math.floor(s%60).toString().padStart(2,'0')}`;
                
                if (!aud || !playBtn) return;

                const disablePlayer = () => {
                    playBtn.disabled = true;
                    seek.disabled = true;
                    repeatBtn.disabled = true;
                    loopBtn.disabled = true;
                    errorDisplay.style.display = 'block';
                    timeDisplay.textContent = "00:00 / 00:00";
                };

                aud.addEventListener('error', disablePlayer);

                aud.addEventListener('loadedmetadata', () => {
                    if (aud.duration === 0 || isNaN(aud.duration)) {
                        disablePlayer();
                    } else {
                        seek.max = aud.duration;
                        timeDisplay.textContent = `00:00 / ${formatTime(aud.duration)}`;
                    }
                });
                
                playBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    if (aud.paused) { aud.play(); playBtn.innerHTML = '⏸'; }
                    else { aud.pause(); playBtn.innerHTML = '▶'; }
                });
                
                repeatBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    repeatOnce = !repeatOnce;
                    repeatBtn.classList.toggle('active', repeatOnce);
                    if (repeatOnce) { aud.loop = false; loopBtn.classList.remove('active'); }
                });
                
                loopBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    aud.loop = !aud.loop;
                    loopBtn.classList.toggle('active', aud.loop);
                    if (aud.loop) { repeatOnce = false; repeatBtn.classList.remove('active'); }
                });
                
                aud.addEventListener('timeupdate', () => {
                    seek.value = aud.currentTime;
                    timeDisplay.textContent = `${formatTime(aud.currentTime)} / ${formatTime(aud.duration)}`;
                });
                
                seek.addEventListener('input', () => { aud.currentTime = parseFloat(seek.value); });
                
                aud.addEventListener('ended', () => {
                    if (repeatOnce) {
                        aud.currentTime = 0; aud.play();
                        repeatOnce = false; repeatBtn.classList.remove('active');
                    } else { playBtn.innerHTML = '▶'; }
                });
            }, 0);
        }

        function applyFilters() { renderGallery(); }

        function toggleFilter() {
            const filterBox = document.getElementById('filter-box');
            const toggle = document.getElementById('filter-toggle');
            filterBox.classList.toggle('collapsed');
            toggle.innerHTML = filterBox.classList.contains('collapsed') ? '&gt;' : '&lt;';
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', loadGallery);
        document.getElementById('jump-id-input')?.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') executeJump();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

(CONTENT END)

    <script>
        const SUPABASE_URL = "https://wtasesmqwpnbwzdynnas.supabase.co";
        const SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = "sb_publishable_ay0PuIePjZwrEgP5XpD5iQ_W5wC-5g9";

        const supabaseClient = supabase.createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_ANON_KEY);

        const MAPPINGS = {
            'casual': 'Casual', 'intermediate': 'Intermediate', 'expert': 'Expert',
            'betterthanyou': 'Better than you', 'obsessed': 'Obsessed', 'loveit': 'Love it',
            'kindofloveit': 'Kind of love it', 'kindofhateit': 'Kind of hate it',
            'ragequitting': 'Rage quitting', 'lfg': 'Looking for group',
            'otp': 'Open to play', 'lft': 'Looking for tips',
            'ott': 'Open to teach', 'ltd': 'Looking to discuss'
        };

        let gamesData = null;
        let isAdmin = false;
        let activeEditIdx = null;
        let dragItemIdx = null;
        let dragCategory = null;

        async function initAuth() {
            const { data: { session } } = await supabaseClient.auth.getSession();
            handleUserSession(session);
            supabaseClient.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
                handleUserSession(session);
            });
        }

        function handleUserSession(session) {
            if (session && session.user && session.user.email.toLowerCase() === '3rr0r.d3v@gmail.com') {
                isAdmin = true;
                document.body.classList.add('is-admin');
            } else {
                isAdmin = false;
                document.body.classList.remove('is-admin');
            }
            if (gamesData) renderPage();
        }

        async function initDatabase() {
            const { data, error } = await supabaseClient
                .from('site_content')
                .select('data')
                .eq('key', 'games')
                .single();

            if (data && data.data) {
                gamesData = data.data;
                renderPage();
            }

            supabaseClient
                .channel('games-realtime')
                .on(
                    'postgres_changes',
                    { event: 'UPDATE', schema: 'public', table: 'site_content', filter: 'key=eq.games' },
                    (payload) => {
                        if (payload.new && payload.new.data) {
                            gamesData = payload.new.data;
                            renderPage();
                        }
                    }
                )
                .subscribe();
        }

        async function syncToSupabase() {
            if (!isAdmin) return;
            const { error } = await supabaseClient
                .from('site_content')
                .update({ data: gamesData })
                .eq('key', 'games');
            if (error) {
                alert("Error saving: " + error.message);
            }
        }

        function renderPage() {
            renderFavorites(gamesData.favorites);
            renderGrid(gamesData.liked, 'liked-games-grid', 'liked');
            renderGrid(gamesData.wanttoplay, 'wtp-games-grid', 'wanttoplay');
        }

        function renderFavorites(favs) {
            const container = document.getElementById('favorite-list');
            container.innerHTML = '';
            if (!favs) return;
            favs.forEach((game, idx) => {
                let tagsHTML = '';
                if (game.tags.skill?.display) tagsHTML += `<span class="tag-box tag-skill">${MAPPINGS[game.tags.skill.level] || game.tags.skill.level}</span>`;
                if (game.tags.rating?.display) tagsHTML += `<span class="tag-box tag-rating">${MAPPINGS[game.tags.rating.rating] || game.tags.rating.rating}</span>`;
                if (game.tags.lf?.display) tagsHTML += `<span class="tag-box tag-lf">${MAPPINGS[game.tags.lf.looking] || game.tags.lf.looking}</span>`;
                
                const inner = `
                    <button class="admin-action-btn" id="edit-fav-btn-${idx}" style="top:4px; left:4px;">✎</button>
                    <button class="admin-action-btn del-btn" id="del-fav-btn-${idx}" style="top:4px; right:4px;">✕</button>
                    <div class="fav-info-group">
                        <div class="fav-title">${game.title}</div>
                        ${game.comment ? `<span class="fav-comment">${game.comment}</span>` : ''}
                    </div>
                    <div class="fav-tags">${tagsHTML}</div>
                `;
                
                const wrap = createTiltWrapper('fav-card', inner);
                wrap.dataset.index = idx;
                
                if (isAdmin) {
                    wrap.draggable = true;
                    wrap.addEventListener('dragstart', (e) => {
                        dragItemIdx = idx;
                        dragCategory = 'favorites';
                        e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
                    });
                    wrap.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
                        if (dragCategory !== 'favorites') return;
                        e.preventDefault();
                    });
                    wrap.addEventListener('drop', async (e) => {
                        if (dragCategory !== 'favorites') return;
                        e.preventDefault();
                        const targetIdx = idx;
                        if (dragItemIdx === targetIdx) return;
                        const [reorderedItem] = gamesData.favorites.splice(dragItemIdx, 1);
                        gamesData.favorites.splice(targetIdx, 0, reorderedItem);
                        await syncToSupabase();
                    });
                }

                container.appendChild(wrap);

                const delBtn = document.getElementById(`del-fav-btn-${idx}`);
                if (delBtn) {
                    delBtn.onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); deleteFavorite(idx); };
                }

                const editBtn = document.getElementById(`edit-fav-btn-${idx}`);
                if (editBtn) {
                    editBtn.onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); openEditFavModal(game, idx); };
                }
            });
        }

        function renderGrid(list, containerId, categoryKey) {
            const grid = document.getElementById(containerId);
            grid.innerHTML = '';
            if (!list) return;
            list.forEach((title, idx) => {
                const inner = `
                    <button class="admin-action-btn" style="top:5px; left:5px; font-size:10px;" id="grid-edit-${categoryKey}-${idx}">✎</button>
                    <button class="admin-action-btn del-btn" style="top:5px; right:5px; font-size:10px;" id="grid-del-${categoryKey}-${idx}">✕</button>
                    ${title}
                `;
                
                const wrap = createTiltWrapper('liked-card', inner);
                wrap.dataset.index = idx;
                
                if (isAdmin) {
                    wrap.draggable = true;
                    wrap.addEventListener('dragstart', (e) => {
                        dragItemIdx = idx;
                        dragCategory = categoryKey;
                        e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
                    });
                    wrap.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => {
                        if (dragCategory !== categoryKey) return;
                        e.preventDefault();
                    });
                    wrap.addEventListener('drop', async (e) => {
                        if (dragCategory !== categoryKey) return;
                        e.preventDefault();
                        const targetIdx = idx;
                        if (dragItemIdx === targetIdx) return;
                        const listArr = categoryKey === 'liked' ? gamesData.liked : gamesData.wanttoplay;
                        const [reorderedItem] = listArr.splice(dragItemIdx, 1);
                        listArr.splice(targetIdx, 0, reorderedItem);
                        await syncToSupabase();
                    });
                }

                grid.appendChild(wrap);

                const delBtn = document.getElementById(`grid-del-${categoryKey}-${idx}`);
                if (delBtn) {
                    delBtn.onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); deleteGridItem(categoryKey, idx); };
                }

                const editBtn = document.getElementById(`grid-edit-${categoryKey}-${idx}`);
                if (editBtn) {
                    editBtn.onclick = (e) => { e.stopPropagation(); editGridItem(categoryKey, idx); };
                }
            });
            document.querySelectorAll('.liked-card').forEach(fitText);
        }

        function randomizeTags(wrapper) {
            const tags = wrapper.querySelectorAll('.tag-box');
            tags.forEach(tag => {
                const z = Math.floor(Math.random() * 50) + 30;
                const y = Math.floor(Math.random() * 12) * -1;
                const r = Math.floor(Math.random() * 24) - 12;
                tag.style.setProperty('--rand-z', `${z}px`);
                tag.style.setProperty('--rand-y', `${y}px`);
                tag.style.setProperty('--rand-r', `${r}deg`);
            });
        }

        function handleTilt(e) {
            const wrapper = e.currentTarget;
            const card = wrapper.querySelector('.fav-card, .liked-card');
            const rect = wrapper.getBoundingClientRect();
            const clientX = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
            const clientY = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientY : e.clientY;
            const x = clientX - rect.left;
            const y = clientY - rect.top;
            const centerX = rect.width / 2;
            const centerY = rect.height / 2;
            let rotX, rotY, scale;

            if (card.classList.contains('fav-card')) {
                rotX = (centerY - y) / 15; 
                rotY = (x - centerX) / 80; 
                rotX = Math.max(Math.min(rotX, 7), -7);
                rotY = Math.max(Math.min(rotY, 7), -7);
                scale = 1.03;
            } else {
                rotX = (centerY - y) / 6; 
                rotY = (x - centerX) / 10;
                scale = 1.1;
            }
            card.style.transform = `rotateX(${rotX}deg) rotateY(${rotY}deg) scale3d(${scale}, ${scale}, ${scale})`;
        }

        function resetAllTilts() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.fav-card, .liked-card').forEach(card => {
                card.style.transform = `rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) scale3d(1, 1, 1)`;
                card.parentElement.classList.remove('is-tapped');
            });
        }

        function createTiltWrapper(contentClass, innerHTML) {
            const wrap = document.createElement('div');
            wrap.className = 'tilt-wrapper';
            wrap.innerHTML = `<div class="${contentClass}">${innerHTML}</div>`;
            const startInteraction = () => {
                if (contentClass === 'fav-card') randomizeTags(wrap);
                wrap.classList.add('is-tapped');
            };

            wrap.addEventListener('mouseenter', startInteraction);
            wrap.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
                resetAllTilts();
                startInteraction();
                handleTilt(e);
            }, {passive: true});

            wrap.addEventListener('mousemove', handleTilt);
            wrap.addEventListener('touchmove', handleTilt, {passive: true});
            wrap.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                const card = wrap.querySelector('.fav-card, .liked-card');
                card.style.transform = `rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) scale3d(1, 1, 1)`;
                wrap.classList.remove('is-tapped');
            });
            return wrap;
        }

        function fitText(el) {
            let fontSize = 0.85;
            el.style.fontSize = fontSize + 'rem';
            while (el.scrollHeight > el.offsetHeight && fontSize > 0.5) {
                fontSize -= 0.02;
                el.style.fontSize = fontSize + 'rem';
            }
        }

        window.toggleSelectState = (key) => {
            const displayChecked = document.getElementById(`fav-${key}-display`).checked;
            let el;
            if (key === 'skill') el = document.getElementById('fav-skill-level');
            else if (key === 'rating') el = document.getElementById('fav-rating-value');
            else if (key === 'lf') el = document.getElementById('fav-lf-value');
            if (el) el.disabled = !displayChecked;
        };

        window.openAddFavModal = () => {
            activeEditIdx = null;
            document.getElementById('modal-title-label').textContent = "Add Favorite Game";
            document.getElementById('fav-title-input').value = '';
            document.getElementById('fav-comment-input').value = '';
            document.getElementById('fav-skill-display').checked = false;
            document.getElementById('fav-rating-display').checked = false;
            document.getElementById('fav-lf-display').checked = false;
            toggleSelectState('skill');
            toggleSelectState('rating');
            toggleSelectState('lf');
            document.getElementById('fav-modal').classList.add('active');
        };

        function openEditFavModal(game, idx) {
            activeEditIdx = idx;
            document.getElementById('modal-title-label').textContent = "Edit Favorite Game";
            document.getElementById('fav-title-input').value = game.title;
            document.getElementById('fav-comment-input').value = game.comment || '';
            document.getElementById('fav-skill-display').checked = game.tags.skill?.display || false;
            document.getElementById('fav-skill-level').value = game.tags.skill?.level || 'casual';
            document.getElementById('fav-rating-display').checked = game.tags.rating?.display || false;
            document.getElementById('fav-rating-value').value = game.tags.rating?.rating || 'loveit';
            document.getElementById('fav-lf-display').checked = game.tags.lf?.display || false;
            document.getElementById('fav-lf-value').value = game.tags.lf?.looking || 'lfg';
            toggleSelectState('skill');
            toggleSelectState('rating');
            toggleSelectState('lf');
            document.getElementById('fav-modal').classList.add('active');
        }

        window.closeFavModal = () => {
            document.getElementById('fav-modal').classList.remove('active');
        };

        window.saveFavorite = async () => {
            const title = document.getElementById('fav-title-input').value.trim();
            const comment = document.getElementById('fav-comment-input').value.trim();
            if (!title) return;

            const favObj = {
                title,
                comment,
                tags: {
                    skill: {
                        display: document.getElementById('fav-skill-display').checked,
                        level: document.getElementById('fav-skill-level').value
                    },
                    rating: {
                        display: document.getElementById('fav-rating-display').checked,
                        rating: document.getElementById('fav-rating-value').value
                    },
                    lf: {
                        display: document.getElementById('fav-lf-display').checked,
                        looking: document.getElementById('fav-lf-value').value
                    }
                }
            };

            if (activeEditIdx !== null) {
                gamesData.favorites[activeEditIdx] = favObj;
            } else {
                gamesData.favorites.push(favObj);
            }

            closeFavModal();
            await syncToSupabase();
        };

        async function deleteFavorite(idx) {
            if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to delete this favorite game?`)) return;
            gamesData.favorites = gamesData.favorites.filter((_, i) => i !== idx);
            await syncToSupabase();
        }

        window.addGridItem = async (categoryKey) => {
            const input = document.getElementById(categoryKey === 'liked' ? 'add-liked-input' : 'add-wtp-input');
            const val = input.value.trim();
            if (!val) return;
            if (categoryKey === 'liked') {
                gamesData.liked.push(val);
            } else {
                gamesData.wanttoplay.push(val);
            }
            input.value = '';
            await syncToSupabase();
        };

        async function deleteGridItem(categoryKey, idx) {
            if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to delete this item?`)) return;
            if (categoryKey === 'liked') {
                gamesData.liked = gamesData.liked.filter((_, i) => i !== idx);
            } else {
                gamesData.wanttoplay = gamesData.wanttoplay.filter((_, i) => i !== idx);
            }
            await syncToSupabase();
        }

        window.editGridItem = async (categoryKey, idx) => {
            const listArr = categoryKey === 'liked' ? gamesData.liked : gamesData.wanttoplay;
            const newVal = prompt("Edit Game Title:", listArr[idx]);
            if (newVal !== null && newVal.trim() !== '') {
                listArr[idx] = newVal.trim();
                await syncToSupabase();
            }
        };

        document.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
            if (!e.target.closest('.tilt-wrapper')) {
                resetAllTilts();
            }
        }, {passive: true});

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            initDatabase();
            initAuth();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

(CONTENT END)

    <!-- Biography Modal -->
